Current Affairs Commentary

The Current Stage of the Abyssinian Crisis

— Ang

The resolution passed by the League of Nations Council regarding the Abyssinian issue, analyzed, yields four key points: First, based on the resolution of May 25th of this year, and in accordance with Article 5 of the 1928 Italo-Ethiopian Treaty, to continue its arbitration work. This is the fundamental principle of the League of Nations in handling this case. Compared to the situation in May, there seems to be no change today. Second, the Arbitration Committee will not allow disputes regarding the sovereignty of the Walwal area. This is a victory for Mussolini's claim. Third, to immediately appoint the fifth arbitrator. This is the implementation of the League of Nations' resolution from May. Fourth, to convene the League of Nations Council on September 4th of this year to either review the results of the arbitration or discuss the Abyssinian issue comprehensively. This point has greater implications for the future of the Italo-Ethiopian dispute.

Whether the League of Nations can resolve the Italo-Ethiopian dispute peacefully depends entirely on what attitude and efforts the major powers seeking to eliminate war will take. Therefore, the diplomatic activities of the major powers are even more noteworthy than the League of Nations' situation. Before the opening of the League of Nations Council, representatives of Britain and France jointly stated with the Italian representative that diplomatic negotiations would be held in France based on the 1906 Tripartite Treaty. Although the outcome is unpredictable, this is something that British Ambassador to Italy, Drummond, had repeatedly contacted Mussolini about without success. Now the three countries have reached a consensus. Some say that this is an action outside the scope of the League of Nations, which harms the function of the League of Nations. Others say that Abyssinia is being abandoned, and Britain, France, and Italy are suspected of dividing East Africa. These outside opinions are put aside for now. In short, in this highly volatile and serious situation, leaving room for all parties to negotiate calmly can be considered a glimmer of hope in the peace movement.

As for the United States, which stands outside the situation but has the ability to influence the League of Nations, what is its attitude towards this case? The United States has recently been focused on its domestic recovery movement. It is already taking a wait-and-see approach to the Far East, and it is even less willing to seek trouble in East Africa. Since President Roosevelt announced the Good Neighbor Policy, his attitude has been even more obvious. Africa has always been a European colony, and the raw materials produced in Africa are abundant in Central and South America. The United States has little relationship with Africa, except for the two independent countries of Liberia and Abyssinia. The former is because of the migration of African Americans, where the United States is in the position of protector. The latter is just a slightly diplomatic relationship. As for why Abyssinia has become a problem, it is because Britain and France see it as the meeting point of two routes for north-south development (the Cape Town to Cairo connection plan) and east-west development (the breakthrough plan from Cape Verde to French Somaliland). For Italy, it is the object of its East African monopoly plan. This has no direct relationship with the United States. This is why it does not want to get involved in the vortex. However, the United States shares the same sentiment as Britain and France in maintaining world peace. Therefore, the United States is also willing to put in a little effort in terms of morality and diplomacy. Judging from the replies of US Secretary of State Hull regarding the Kellogg-Briand Pact and Abyssinia, and President Roosevelt's indirect remarks in Washington during the League of Nations meeting, remotely supporting the British side, we can know the objective intention of the United States.

A Japanese Advisor Dies in Sui Bin County; Eight Killed, Seven Wounded

(Changchun) According to a telegram received by the Police Department, the joint Japanese-Manchu army in Suibin County encountered a strong group of "bandits" while suppressing "bandits" in the Luobei County area for three days. After a fierce battle, although the enemy suffered heavy losses, eight people, including Jiro Susaki, a consultant from Niigata Prefecture in Suibin County, were killed, and seven were seriously injured. After receiving this urgent report, a support team was immediately dispatched to pursue the "bandits." (Telecommunications from Dentsu on the 6th)

(Tokyo) According to the Dongbao newspaper, the misfortune on the Jingtu Railway has been occurring since November 17, 1932, when the rebel army attacked Yingchengzi Station. Because the Japanese-Manchu military and police security was very sufficient, there had been no incidents until now. Recently, this misfortune suddenly occurred, and the siege in the evening was a bold and invincible act. Since the beginning of this year, there have been six attacks on trains, all carried out by communist-affiliated rebel armies. Their tactics are very clever, and the road destruction situation is as follows:

March 14th: Attacked Mifeng Station on the Binsui Railway. No casualties.

May 2nd: Attacked Halbaling on the Jingtu Railway. More than 200 Korean communists, nine soldiers and civilians killed, 17 captured.

May 25th: Attacked Yebuluo Station on the Binsui Railway. 300 Chinese, Korean, and Russian allied forces, several casualties.

May 27th: Attacked Xiao Jiu Station on the Binsui Railway. Five wounded, two dead.

June 7th: Attacked Mao'er Mountain on the Binsui Railway. Two killed, 30 captured.

July 21st: Bombed the Mao'er Mountain tracks. Two seriously injured. (Telecommunications from the China United Press on the 6th)

Hurricane in the Philippines

(Manila) A hurricane swept through northern and central Luzon, followed by severe flooding. It is reported that seventeen people have died, and another twenty are missing. Thousands are homeless. Heavy rain is currently pouring down, with no sign of stopping. (Telecommunications from Reuters on the 5th)

Germany's Internal Worries Have Not Ended; Strict Prevention of Opposition Activities; Red Character Banners Raised Throughout Berlin; The Roman Pope Instructs German Religious Followers

(Berlin) Red character banners ten feet high are now displayed throughout the city, with the text: "Germans, listen! Reactionaries are now active. Beware of wolves in sheep's clothing coming to you." This is the latest action in the general movement to eliminate those who oppose the National Socialist Party. Stormtroopers are patrolling the entire city in motorized vehicles at night, shouting slogans to eliminate those who oppose the National Socialist Party. (Telecommunications from Reuters on the 6th)

(Berlin) Propaganda Minister Goebbels today began a campaign against Catholic agitators. At the same time, the court sentenced a Communist Party member to death. The authorities also arrested dozens of Jews for the crime of insulting the race. Today, Goebbels' warning is posted on billboards everywhere, stating: "German people, beware! Do not be deceived by those who wear sheep's clothing." It also claims that Catholics and Communists have a conspiracy against the state. (Telecommunications from the National Press on the 5th)

(Berlin) German Justice Minister Gürtner ordered strict punishment for those who illegally carry firearms, in order to prevent the activities of various groups that are hostile to the state. The order stated that it is not enough to punish only those who illegally carry firearms; it is necessary to investigate the secret organizations that secretly supply the firearms in order to eliminate them all in one fell swoop, and to closely monitor the illegal import of firearms from foreign countries. (Telecommunications from Havas on the 6th)

(Berlin) The German Cultural Association recently notified the cultural and artistic groups of various Jewish organizations to organize the German Jewish Cultural Group Association before August 31. In the future, only groups participating in this association will be allowed to conduct external activities. However, this measure does not include Jewish-run schools and church groups. (Telecommunications from Havas on the 5th)

(Berlin) The court today sentenced the Communist Kiser to death for attempting to treason. (Telecommunications from the National Press on the 5th)

Vatican City: Fifty young religious followers from the German city of Dresden recently came here to meet with the Pope and discussed the recent anti-religious movement in their country. The Pope specifically instructed them, saying, "Some people who advocate new paganism are actually launching a struggle against Jesus. Every time we think about it, we are deeply worried. But when we think about the fact that there are still so many young believers in Germany who are devout and unyielding, we can also be happy. In short, the recent situation in Germany has created a spiritual reflection on me, which is both happy and sad. That's all." The Pope also met with the Archbishop of Berlin, Presing, today to discuss matters. (Telecommunications from Havas on the 5th)

Vatican City: The Pope gave a speech to fifty Germans who came to the Vatican today, saying that he very much wanted to bless all German Catholics because they were still fighting to defend their faith in these very difficult times. However, the Pope also warned the Germans that the situation in the future may be even more difficult. (Telecommunications from the National Press on the 5th)

Britain, France, and Italy to Meet in Paris Next Week to Negotiate the Abyssinian Issue

(London) Preparations are currently underway to begin negotiations between Britain, France, and Italy on the Abyssinian issue in Paris or near Paris early next week. This morning, British Cabinet member Eden reported in detail to Foreign Secretary Hoare on the compromise solution to the Italo-Ethiopian dispute established by the League of Nations Executive Council last week. It is expected that the Ethiopian representatives will not be invited to participate in the initial discussions among the three countries, but the Ethiopian ambassador to France will be notified of the progress of the discussions. At the same time, official circles in London deny that Britain has banned British citizens from serving in Ethiopia. (Telecommunications from Reuters on the 6th)

(Rome) It is reported that Ethiopia insists that the mediation committee study the very drawing of boundary lines, so the committee is now experiencing difficulties. People in Rome believe that if Ethiopia insists on not conceding, then the meeting of the mediation committee convened according to the resolution passed by the League of Nations Executive Council on Saturday and Sunday will be impossible. (Telecommunications from Reuters on the 6th)

Mussolini Again Transfers 70,000 Troops to Africa; Aviation Undersecretary Goes to Inspect the Air Force

(Rome) Although Italy has agreed to abide by the League of Nations' compromise solution regarding the Italo-Ethiopian dispute, it is still actively preparing for war. An order was issued today to recruit another 70,000 soldiers to East Africa, including two divisions of regular troops, one division of Blackshirts, and other troops who will be recruited to replenish domestic forces. At the same time, several ships are currently busy loading goods in preparation for sailing to Africa. (Telecommunications from Reuters on the 6th)

(Rome) Italian Prime Minister Mussolini today also ordered the mobilization of two army divisions to East Africa, one being the "Asiata Division," concentrated in the Adige area, under the command of General Ligarti, and the other being the "Corseria Division," concentrated in the Imperia area, under the command of General Bendor. In addition, Italian volunteers residing abroad and former veterans are led by army students undergoing short-term training to form the Sixth Division of the Fascist Party's army, which is concentrated and awaiting dispatch, with General Pascaldi serving as commander. The mobilization of the above divisions is progressing very well. To date, the total number of Italian troops sent to East Africa has reached twelve divisions. (Telecommunications from Havas on the 6th)

(Rome) Mussolini today again mobilized 65,000 troops to East Africa, stating that although the League of Nations Executive Council has entrusted the Italo-Ethiopian border dispute to arbitration and established a reconciliation solution, the relationship between the two countries remains tense. Italy deems it necessary to continue mobilization in order to prepare for any eventuality. (Telecommunications from the National Press Agency on the 6th)

(Rome) Mussolini, in view of Ethiopia's continuous mobilization of troops, issued the ninth mobilization order this afternoon. This batch of troops includes two divisions, those towards the French border region of the Biteman province. (Telecommunications from the National Press Agency on the 6th)

(Rome) Today, the Italian government again mobilized the "Asiatai Division" and the "Corseria Division" to East Africa, as mentioned in the previous telegram from Havas. After these two divisions are sent to East Africa, the total number of Italian troops in East Africa will reach twelve divisions, including seven army divisions and five Fascist Party army divisions. In addition to the above twelve divisions, the Italian volunteer army residing abroad will now be formed into a Party army division in preparation for deployment to East Africa. According to a report from the "Great War Volunteer Soldiers Association," 2,000 volunteer soldiers have been authorized to go to East Africa, and another 4,000 are requesting to join the army and are still under review. In addition, Count Ciano, the son-in-law of Prime Minister Mussolini and current Minister of Propaganda, will also go to East Africa to take on military duties. It is said that Italy's military preparations in East Africa eased slightly at the end of July, but have recently accelerated again. The Italian government believes that even if the three-nation meeting of Britain, France, and Italy is held in accordance with the 1906 treaty to resolve the Italo-Ethiopian issue, it may not yield satisfactory results. And even if an agreement is reached between the three countries allowing Italy to develop its economic power in Ethiopia, it is necessary to increase security in East Africa in order to protect Italy's economic interests. This is why Italy continues to send troops to East Africa. (Telecommunications from Havas on the 6th)

(Rome) Air Force Undersecretary General Valle recently flew to Italian Eritrea in East Africa to inspect the Air Force, with an average flight speed of 350 kilometers per hour and a flight altitude of approximately 4,500 meters. On the return journey, he departed from the port of Massawa at 5:00 a.m., made a brief stop in Cairo, Egypt, and arrived in Rome at 5:45 p.m. (Telecommunications from Havas on the 6th)

Ethiopia Still Fears Italian Military Preparations; Cables Thanks to Various Countries for Upholding Peace; The Ethiopian Emperor Receives the US Representative

Addis Ababa: The news of the League of Nations Executive Council's passage of the Italo-Ethiopian dispute resolution has only made people more indignant. They say that Italy can more calmly prepare for war within the month before the Executive Council reconvenes. A senior government official today told a guest that Ethiopia is deeply regretful that Italy has consistently refused to make a declaration not to resort to force. Without this firm declaration from Italy, it will continue to prepare for the long-rumored offensive. At the same time, we sincerely accept the recommendations of the League of Nations, but it is doubtful whether the strength of the League of Nations can make it effective. After receiving the full text of the League of Nations resolution here, a statement was issued stating that the Ethiopian government is very satisfied with the League of Nations Executive Council's decision to hold a meeting on September 4 to conduct a comprehensive review of all aspects of Italo-Ethiopian relations, as the Ethiopian government has never slackened in its request for such a review to be conducted in the past eight months. (Telecommunications from Reuters on the 5th)

Addis Ababa: The Ethiopian Emperor formally received US Chargé d'Affaires Angerde today. At that time, the Ethiopian Emperor expressed his gratitude to Angerde for President Roosevelt's statement last week and called it an example of the American people's love of peace. He also praised the work of American clergymen in Ethiopia. (Telecommunications from the National Press on the 5th)

(Geneva) The Ethiopian Emperor sent a telegram to the League of Nations Executive Council today, expressing his thanks to various countries for their efforts to maintain peace in East Africa, and stated that he is determined to achieve a just and peaceful resolution to the Italo-Ethiopian dispute. (Telecommunications from the National Press on the 5th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Secretariat received a thank-you telegram from the Ethiopian Emperor on the 4th, urging them to express his thanks to the representatives of various countries who worked hard to pass the Executive Council's resolution, and stated that the Ethiopian government reaffirms its determination to resolve this dispute peacefully and fairly, hoping that the League of Nations will make every effort to achieve peace. (Telecommunications from the National Press on the 5th)

Addis Ababa: The Ministry of Foreign Affairs recently issued a press release regarding the resolution passed by the League of Nations Executive Council the other day: "The Ethiopian government has just read the two resolutions passed by the League of Nations Executive Council on August 3. The issue of responsibility for the Walwal incident will be decided by the fifth arbitrator. According to the first resolution of the Executive Council, it seems possible to arbitrate the two disputed encounters, but no matter how the arbitration committee decides, the fact that Walwal was drawn within Ethiopian territory on the official maps drawn by Italy can hardly be concealed. As for the memorandum previously submitted by Italy, it only points out that the current Walwal has been substantially occupied by Italian troops. As for the second resolution of the Executive Council, which stipulates that the Executive Council will hold a meeting on September 4 to conduct a comprehensive consideration of the Italo-Ethiopian dispute, this action is sufficient to fully satisfy the Ethiopian government, as the Ethiopian Emperor has requested the Executive Council to handle the Italo-Ethiopian dispute for eight months now, and this policy has remained unchanged." (Telecommunications from Havas on the 5th)

Addis Ababa: A statement was issued here today criticizing the League of Nations Executive Council's resolution on the Italo-Ethiopian issue this time, stating that Walwal is within Ethiopian territory, which is clearly marked on Italian maps, and that Italy issued a memorandum to Ethiopia several years ago stating that Walwal was occupied by Italian troops, which further shows that Walwal is Ethiopian territory. The arbitration committee should not completely disregard this point. The statement expressed satisfaction with the third resolution of the Executive Council, as Ethiopia's request for the study of the entire conflict issue has been for eight months now. However, the statement did not mention the three-power conference based on the 1906 treaty, apparently due to Ethiopia's suspicion of this treaty. According to government sources, Ethiopia cannot recognize any economic concessions beyond what it has previously allowed, and political concessions are even out of the question. Also, one Turkish military officer here, said to have obtained permission from his home government, will serve as a military advisor to the Ethiopian government, and the Ethiopian authorities have accepted. (Telecommunications from the National Press on the 6th)

Japanese Foreign Ministry Denies Selling Arms to Ethiopia

(Tokyo) In response to reports from London that Japan is supplying arms to Ethiopia, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs issued a statement today clarifying the situation regarding Japanese arms manufacturing in order to avoid misunderstandings abroad. The content of the statement is as follows: The Japanese government has never allowed people to manufacture arms privately. All arms exports must be made through the Taihei Kumiai, and only after obtaining government permission can they be sold abroad. Recently, the Taihei Kumiai has not requested the government to issue export permits for weapons. Therefore, there is no basis for the claim that the Ethiopian government and Japanese merchants have concluded arms contracts. Examining the situation in Ethiopia, the railway from Djibouti to Addis Ababa is under the influence of France and Italy. Therefore, without the permission of France and Italy, it is absolutely impossible in fact to transport arms under Djibouti to Addis Ababa. (Telecommunications from Nihon Rengo on the 6th)

(Tokyo) There are rumors that Ethiopia has signed a contract with Japanese arms dealers to purchase arms, or that Japan will send military advisors to Ethiopia, etc. However, the Army authorities issued a statement on the 6th denying this claim. Japan has private arms manufacturing factories, but the government's supervision is very strict and they are not allowed to sell them abroad freely. To date, no arms dealer has requested the government to allow the sale of arms. The rumors are completely untrue. (Telecommunications from Nihon Rengo on the 6th)

Strike Riots in Crete, Greece Suppressed; Three Dead, Thirty-seven Wounded

Athens: The government has received a telegram from General Bakopulos on the island of Crete, stating that 4,000 strikers looted various administrative agencies, but order has now been restored. He surrounded Candia with troops, and when he demanded the strikers to surrender, they quietly dispersed. He met with a delegation of strikers and listened to their demands. Therefore, they agreed to obey the authorities. It is reported that three people died and twenty were injured during the conflict between the strikers and the military police, and seventeen soldiers were also injured. After the riots broke out, armed police rushed to suppress them and declared martial law. (Telecommunications from Reuters on the 5th)

Athens: The situation on the island of Crete has suddenly become serious. Government agencies have stopped working. The Greek government immediately dispatched two warships to the scene to restore order and declared martial law. It is said that there are a total of 4,000 strikers. When the conflict occurred with the police, a total of 100 people were injured on the workers' side. The Greek fleet is now concentrated near Athens, waiting for orders to depart. It is heard that this incident is directly or indirectly related to the forces of Venizelos. Venizelos is a Cretan, and his party members, in order to promote their political goals, advocate that workers adopt a policy of force. They united with the workers to attack and occupy the town hall. It is heard that Bakoboro, the commander of the defense forces on the island of Crete, and Chief of Police Shedoko were both seriously injured. The Greek government now believes that it can completely restore order within two days. The latest reports claim that the rebels have completely occupied the town of Heraklion and five bombers have now been ordered to depart from Athens. If they encounter resistance from the rebels, they will carry out bombing. (Telecommunications from the National Press on the 5th)

(Paris) The Times believes that the general strike on the island of Crete is a new political movement. The rebels have clashed with government forces multiple times, occupied arsenals, and used the captured weapons to repel the troops. The number of troops is small and unable to resist the thousands of rebels. Army Chief Gondilis ordered the suppression of the rebellion, without mercy. The majority of the defense forces at the Athens airfield also rebelled after hearing about the uprising on the island of Crete. After a fierce battle, it was finally put down. As a result, fifteen rebel soldiers were captured and will be tried by a military court. (Telecommunications from the National Press on the 5th)

Athens: It was announced here today that the rebellion in Candia has ended. The strikers have accepted the final warning and surrendered their weapons unconditionally and disbanded. The government had previously accepted the wage demands of the strikers. (Telecommunications from the National Press on the 5th)

Heraklion, Greece: The island of Crete today declared martial law due to the joint disturbance of public order by politically disgruntled elements and labor protesters. The government is taking measures to avoid riots. Originally there was a strike movement in Crete, and in mid-March of this year, the remnants of the revolution that supported former Prime Minister Venizelos seized the opportunity to create difficulties for the government, leading the masses into public agencies. (Telecommunications from the National Press on the 5th)

Athens: Rumors circulating that the government intends to dissolve republican groups have been officially denied. (Telecommunications from Havas on the 6th)

The Puppet State and Outer Mongolia: Exchange of Representatives Issue; Outer Mongolia Only Permits Handling Border Disputes

(Changchun) After the "Manchukuo" Foreign Affairs Office received a reply from Outer Mongolia regarding the handling of Manchu-Mongolian border disputes, it issued the following statement on the 6th: Outer Mongolia responded to Manchukuo's request on July 29th, proposing that if the powers of the representatives are limited to handling border disputes and the representatives are stationed near the border in mutually designated locations, there would be no objection to exchanging representatives. However, as the proposal contained many ambiguous and unreasonable points, the "Manchukuo" representative in Manchuria suggested on the 5th that Outer Mongolia's request to limit the powers of the representatives to handling border disputes be accepted. The representative also specifically indicated the locations where the representatives of both countries would be stationed and further requested the exchange of central representatives to handle matters that could not be resolved locally. (6th Dispatch Telegram)

(Changchun) The main points of the third request made by "Manchukuo" to Outer Mongolia at the Manchuria meeting on the 5th are that the permanent representative offices of the two countries should be divided into central representatives and local representatives. The specific requirements from Manchukuo are as follows:

Although the central representatives are not plenipotentiary ambassadors or formal diplomatic organs of the two countries like ambassadors, they must, in substance, be representative organs of the two governments, permanently stationed in Changchun and Kulun to handle friendly relations and diplomatic negotiations between the two countries; (2) Local representatives are solely responsible for handling border disputes, permanently stationed in two locations near the border, with "Manchukuo" representatives stationed in Outer Mongolia and Outer Mongolian representatives stationed in "Manchukuo," with the intention of fundamentally resolving the long-standing border issues between the two countries, and further hoping to restore normal diplomatic relations between Manchukuo and Mongolia. (6th Dispatch Telegram)

(Moscow) A Kulun dispatch states that Manchukuo made a further proposal to Mongolia on July 17th. On July 29th, Sambuu presented the Mongolian reply to Ganji, the representative of the Manchukuo Foreign Affairs Department. The reply stated that Mongolia had previously suggested establishing a permanent joint committee to arbitrate border disputes. However, in its reply, Manchukuo issued an ultimatum demanding that Manchukuo representatives be allowed to reside in Mongolian territory at locations chosen by Manchukuo. Otherwise, Mongolian border troops must be completely withdrawn. Mongolia refused to accept these demands, as they infringed upon Mongolian sovereignty and were a direct insult.

Mongolia acknowledges that in the proposal made by Manchukuo on July 17th, it no longer insisted on unilaterally dispatching representatives, but suggested exchanging plenipotentiary representatives. In order to assist in maintaining border peace, Mongolia believes that if the representatives' powers are limited to resolving border issues and their locations are designated by their respective governments near the border to allow for rapid and active intervention when border disputes reoccur, then Mongolia would not object. Mongolia further believes that these representatives should also serve as joint chair representatives on the Border Committee. Mongolia proposed the establishment of the Border Committee, and Manchukuo did not object. (6th TASS Dispatch)

Matsuoka's Future Mission: Reorganize the South Manchuria Railway to Promote Economic Development in China

The Japanese-language Manchuria Daily reported on the 2nd of this month that since Count Hayashi Hirotaro resigned and it was decided that Matsuoka Yosuke would succeed him, a wave of change has swept through the South Manchuria Railway Company, both internally and externally. Matsuoka Yosuke has been widely noticed since his activities in Geneva. How Matsuoka will build his foundation in the domestic political world and how Matsuoka will decide to guide the future of the South Manchuria Railway Company have become the focus of attention within the company. According to most observers, the focus will be on resolving the reorganization of the South Manchuria Railway Company and expanding economic work in China. It is recalled that the issue of reorganizing the South Manchuria Railway Company has been stalled since the local plan was submitted to the central government in December of Showa 8 (1933). However, the South Manchuria Railway Company itself also believes that after the Incident, it should adapt to the new situation and undergo reforms. This is also a long-standing desire of the military. However, implementing this major issue requires a person with great vision, credibility in all aspects, and who is trusted by the company. Matsuoka is well-suited for this task because he has gained the favor of the military. As for the reorganization issue, there are four main points: (1) Whether railway control is possible; (2) Whether coal mine separation is possible; (3) Whether the establishment of a new trading company is possible; (4) Whether the transfer of local administration is possible. The fourth point has been decided to be newly established, but it is still pending implementation. It will be implemented after the new president makes a decision on the transfer of local administration. The transfer of local administration has been a long-standing issue that has not been resolved for many years. Matsuoka has expressed his view on this issue, advocating the pure economic organization of the South Manchuria Railway, advocating transfer, and also advocating the abolition of extraterritoriality and the transfer of affiliated lands. Therefore, it is only a matter of time. The most difficult aspects are the railway and coal mine issues. If the two are separated, the South Manchuria Railway will undergo a major transformation. If they are not separated, the degree of reform will be relatively minor. Furthermore, the integration of the Railway Department and the General Bureau's finances has, in fact, become a new railway company. This is now gradually coming to the surface. However, harmonizing the contradictions between the Railway Department and the General Bureau, while also making the entire Manchurian railway organically operated, requires the decision of the new president. As for the second step, the expansion of economic work in China relies on Matsuoka's skills. Matsuoka had aspirations when he was a director. Now that the situation in North China has changed, Matsuoka can observe inside and outside the company and develop his plans. In particular, the procurement of funds is an important issue for the South Manchuria Railway in the future. To obtain new funds, it is necessary to expand the limits of corporate bonds. However, this year's corporate bond plan has encountered various difficulties. The new President Matsuoka may be able to obtain assistance from the central government to manage reasonably and procure funds.

Japan's Seiyukai Party Decides on New Policies

(Tokyo) In preparation for the upcoming prefectural assembly elections and general elections, the Seiyukai held a joint meeting of executives and policy research staff on the 6th and decided on new policies. The main points are summarized below: (1) The National Essence Issue: The fundamental meaning of the national polity is the unchanging belief of the people. Any words or actions that disrupt or violate the so-called Emperor Organ Theory cannot be tolerated in the slightest. (2) National Policy Issues: In view of the world situation and Japan's position, the extraordinary circumstances of the times have become even more serious. National defense and industry urgently need to seek a mutually beneficial policy, while maintaining, developing, and improving the welfare of the middle class is the core of domestic national policy. (3) Policy Issues: Recently, the government authorities have only focused on adhering to financial arrangements and have not paid attention to the implementation of national policies. The following are the strategies for balancing national defense and industry and maintaining and developing the middle class: (A) Expect the strengthening of national defense and pay special attention to its economization. (B) Seek to adjust the economy with "Manchukuo" and actively cooperate with China. (C) Establish a local financial subsidy system. (D) In order to develop industry and maintain the middle class, thoroughly lower interest rates and create diversified institutions for people's finance to expand the debt reorganization system. (E) Re-examine the expenditures of national finances, and seek to make the public bonds that must be reorganized more accessible to the people. As for the investment relations of the general financial market with Manchuria and China, efforts must also be made to adjust them. (6th Japan League Dispatch)

US Magazine Parodies the Japanese Emperor; Hull Regrets But Does Not Take Responsibility; Japan Has Not Yet Decided Whether to Officially Protest; Cartoonist Welcomes Japan's Entry Ban

(Washington) Japanese Ambassador to the United States Saito today negotiated with the State Department regarding a magazine cartoon, saying that the cartoon insulted the Japanese Emperor and the Japanese people. Secretary of State Hull replied that the matter was regrettable, but the US government does not have the power to censor newspapers and therefore is not responsible for any publications. Saito has not been able to declare that he will formally protest the cartoon until it has been discussed in detail in Tokyo. The Japanese seem to be dissatisfied not with the satire of the peace prize depicted in the cartoon, but with the degradation of depicting the Emperor dragging a cannon. The cartoonist is Mr. Gropper. Gropper says that the Emperor should see the other cartoons he has drawn. Newspapers carrying his cartoons have already been banned from entering several countries, including Germany. If Japan also joins the ranks of those who oppose his cartoons, he will be very happy. The opponents currently include one labor leader, several capitalists, and an emperor. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

(Washington) Japanese Ambassador to the United States Saito today informally negotiated with Secretary of State Hull about the incident of an American game magazine publishing a satirical cartoon disrespectful of the Japanese Emperor. After the meeting, the Japanese Ambassador believed that he had received a direct expression of apology from Hull. However, it was also learned that Hull had tried to avoid a direct expression, only saying that he was very unhappy that the satire had been misunderstood in Japan. The official statement from the State Department stated, "When the Secretary of State replied to the Japanese Ambassador, he reported to the Ambassador that the publisher of the magazine had stated that there was no intention to offend, and that he was always unhappy about such things causing misunderstandings." According to Gropper, the artist who drew the satire, he intended to attack Japanese imperialism, and he does not care how the Japanese react. (5th National Telegram)

Japan Negotiates with South Africa to Revoke High Tariff Case

(Tokyo) In order to prevent the import of Japanese goods, the Union of South Africa has promulgated a new tariff law of three yuan, imposing heavy taxes on Japanese cotton yarn, pottery, glass, etc. The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs sent a telegram to Consul Fujimura with three major points, instructing him to contact the South African government authorities and urge them to cancel the special tariffs on Japan. The contents of the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs' instruction are as follows:

(1) Japan is trying to adjust the one-sided trade with South Africa.

(2) Last year, South African wool was 20 yuan more expensive than Australian wool, and Japan was willing to suffer losses to order 20,000 bales of wool from South Africa. This was Japan's effort to adjust. This year, because the price difference is 70 yuan, it is impossible to sell more. However, 7,000 bales have already been purchased, and more purchases of South African wool are being considered next year.

(3) Japan has organized an export association to South Africa and is determined to implement trade restrictions.

Japan urges the South African authorities to reflect on these three points and abolish the new tariff rules. (6th China United Press Dispatch)

Upon their return, 700 British war veterans gathered today to welcome them. We gained a lot during our travels in Germany. This experience will be very useful. It should be known that the governments of all countries in the world are genuinely committed to peace and do not risk the collapse of their government positions. I believe that we have now opened the way for peace efforts and achieved success. I dare to believe that German war veterans all agree to be friends with us." If this is ineffective, then measures will be determined. (Washington) Today, the House of Representatives passed President Roosevelt's wealth tax bill by a vote of 282 to 96. The bill includes inheritance tax, gift tax, personal income tax, and corporate store profit tax. It also includes severe penalties for non-compliance. The bill is largely in line with Roosevelt's original proposal, except that the income of charitable organizations is exempt by five percent. (5th National News Agency Dispatch)

The Average Lifespan of Japanese People Still Has Not Reached 50 Years

(Tokyo) The Cabinet Statistics Bureau announced the latest survey on the lifespan of Japanese people on the 6th. It is said that since ancient times, "life is no more than fifty years" has become a popular saying. However, in reality, the average lifespan of Japanese men is only slightly less than 45 years, and the average lifespan of Japanese women is only slightly less than 47 years, which is still far from the "fifty years" of lifespan mentioned in the saying. Compared to the previous announcement, the lifespan of men is shortened every year, but women live longer than men. The death rate of Japanese people is the highest compared to countries such as England, America, Germany, France, and Italy, indicating that the health condition of the Japanese people is still inferior. In particular, the high mortality rate in infancy is even more noteworthy. (6th Japan League Dispatch)

(Tokyo) According to a survey by the Japanese Statistics Bureau, based on the national census of 1925 and 1930, the death rate of Japanese people is 20 per thousand. (6th China United Press Dispatch)

The boat eventually capsized. Coots and the others clung to rubber mattresses and floated on the sea. They eventually managed to make their way ashore, but spent the night exposed on the island. They had no food and no clothes to change into. It was not until this morning that they were spotted by a local boat, which took them back to Hong Kong. Although they were badly frightened, they were all unharmed. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

Yan Xishan Advocates Inter-Provincial Exchange of Goods

(Nanjing) Yan Xishan, the Pacification Commissioner of Taiyuan, believes that since most of Shanxi's commercial goods come from outside the province, it leads to annual trade deficits. When Shanxi people's overseas business was developed, there was an inflow of forty to fifty million in working capital, so it could barely be supported. Recently, the sharp decrease in foreign exchange has caused the province's economy to be extremely exhausted. In addition to issuing local currency in the province to promote the purchase of provincial goods, he is also implementing inter-provincial exchange of goods. He has dispatched technician Ye from the Construction Department to the south to first contact the Zhejiang Provincial Government to exchange Shanxi's wool, sheepskin, carpets, and all other handmade specialty products for Zhejiang's silk and low-priced daily necessities. After the two parties negotiate a compromise, Ye will go to Zhenjiang to contact the Jiangsu Construction Department. However, the categories still need to be inspected by both parties based on their needs before opening a list for mutual reference. Ye's mission has been completed, and he took the Jinpu train north on the morning of the 6th to return to Shanxi to report. Afterwards, he will continue to visit Henan, Hubei, Hunan, and other provinces to make similar contacts. It is heard that Yan's proposed exchange of goods method uses the value of the goods as the standard, and the exchange center is the Provincial Bank or the bank designated as the agent Provincial Treasury. If the promotion is smooth, it will be implemented in the same way with all provinces across the country, so that domestic goods can circulate in large quantities and money will not flow out. In order to seek all conveniences, Yan has already sent a telegram to the Central Government and distributed it to the Ministries of Industry, Railways, and Finance. In addition to detailing the contents of the method, he requested that the transportation fees be reduced during transportation and that the transit tax be reduced or exempted during transit to show promotion. Large-Scale Bandit Suppression in Hebei Province Liu Guitang's Bandits Harass the War Zone

Tianjin Correspondence: In the past month, due to the changes in the political situation in Hebei, the troop movements, and the emptiness of local defenses, and at a time when green gauze screens are rising, bandits in various places have taken the opportunity to become active. The bandit atmosphere is particularly strong in Wen'an, Baxian, Anci, Jinghai, Renqiu, and other counties. The bandits often rely on dense reeds as a barrier, appearing and disappearing unpredictably, and repeatedly suppressing police groups. Dong Ze's gang in Wen'an and Baxian has gathered as many as a thousand people. Since mid-last month, they have resisted the bandit suppression troops, and the problem has not yet been resolved. Recently, the Tang and Liang regiments of the 141st Division of the 32nd Army, together with the militia of Wen'an and Baxian counties, have divided into nine routes, surrounding the reed pond where Dong's bandits are hiding, and implementing a long-term encirclement method to starve the bandits. They also gathered brave civilians to cut down the reeds, so that the bandits lose their barrier, in order to sweep them away in one fell swoop. Therefore, this branch of bandits is difficult to pacify effectively in a short time. Shengfang Town, Jinghai County, was also occupied by bandits before. Up until last week, the Five Rivers Water Public Security Bureau dispatched over twenty patrol boats, and the Song Division troops of the 32nd Army attacked by land and water, and the bandits began to flee along the South Canal, abandoning over twenty hostages. They were escorted back to their hometowns by the military police. However, although the bandits fled, their strength has not been eliminated. There have been reports recently that they are entrenched in Yangliuqing. The province plans to divide the entire province into three areas (excluding the war zone) and search and suppress them along the east, south, and west routes. The east area is centered on Jinghai, Wen'an, Baxian, Renqiu, and other counties. The west area is centered on Huolu, Lingshou, and Quyang. The south area is centered on Daming, Xingtai, and Handan. The 32nd Army of Shang Zhen's department will dispatch two divisions to cooperate with the local security teams and militia, and be organized into three major guerrilla teams, under the command of the Provincial Security Office. Shang Zhen also plans to personally command one area when necessary, along with Li Peiji, Director of the Civil Affairs Department, and Li Xingcun, Deputy Director of the Provincial Security Office, leading the team to suppress them. Currently, in all 130 counties of Hebei Province, the bandit atmosphere is rampant in over sixty counties. There has been excessive rainfall this year, and the rivers have overflowed. If the bandits are not suppressed, everyone will hardly survive.

The bandits in the war zone have also suddenly become active in the past half month. Outside the various passes of the Great Wall, bandits have gathered four to five thousand people. They recently attacked Taipingzhai and Luotun, near Qian'an County, and Walong Mountain in Lulong County. Even Panjiakou and Xifengkou were once occupied by bandits. Zhang Yantian, the commander of the Second Security Brigade, was ordered to lead his troops to suppress them. However, the bandits are rampant and numerous, and they flee as they are suppressed, so they have not been successful. Yin Rugeng, the Administrative Inspector of the Lianyuyu District, plans to convene a meeting of the heads of the security brigades and county magistrates in the jurisdiction after taking office, and then decide on a large-scale clean-up method. However, the bandits in that area are the old troops of Liu Guitang, who have been secretly training outside the pass for half a year. They are currently commanded by Bai Jianwu and Lin Yulin. There are also many near Xinglong Ping'an Fort and Gubeikou. The team of Liu Guitang hiding between Yuguan and Shihe has about six to seven hundred persons. The bandits claimed to have obtained the understanding of the Japanese Kwantung Army and the North China Garrison and intend to occupy the war zone, so they openly unveiled the false flag of the "North China Autonomous National Salvation Army". The firearms are well equipped, and there are heavy weapons such as machine guns and field guns. The Gubeikou Japanese military Kawakishi Brigade Headquarters specifically ordered staff officer Harada last week to visit Huo Shi, director of the Gubeikou Office of the Jimi Administrative Region, and deliver a statement, which stated, "Liu Bai and other troublemakers hold business cards of our army's officers and are using our army's name, and there are Japanese ronin participating in it, claiming to have contacted the enemy army. After investigation, it is confirmed that they have absolutely no relationship with our Tianjin Garrison and the Kwantung Army. Our army is extremely indignant about this. Please take decisive measures and thoroughly suppress these troublemakers who obstruct Sino-Japanese relations. In the event that your special police force is weak, please notify our army to jointly assist in the suppression, so as to thoroughly eliminate the troublemakers who obstruct Sino-Japanese relations." (4th)

Western River Counties of Guangdong Province: Rushing to Build Autumn Embankments After the Disaster, Engaging in Autumn Cultivation to Maintain Food Supply, and Distributing Relief Funds to Provide Work Relief

Guangzhou Correspondence: The counties in the western part of Guangdong Province, which suffered from flooding, are now seeing the floodwaters receding daily. However, handling the aftermath requires financial resources everywhere. In addition to raising funds for immediate relief, the relief committees in various counties are also urgently planning to build autumn embankments to address concerns about food shortages. They aim to repair breaches in the dikes and embankments of farmland in the disaster areas to facilitate timely autumn cultivation, thereby preventing a complete failure of the late rice crop. The dike repair project will also employ a large number of refugees, providing work relief, which is a win-win situation. Therefore, rushing to build autumn embankments in the disaster areas is currently a top priority. However, initiating construction projects requires funding, and the county relief committees have repeatedly appealed to the government for the prompt allocation of relief funds to enable these projects. Finally, on July 30th, the provincial government approved the distribution plan for the Northwest River flood relief funds. The Finance Department will allocate 100,000 yuan as requested, instructing each county to send representatives to the provincial capital to receive the funds. According to the distribution plan, Gaoyao County is allocated 20,000 yuan, with 18,000 yuan for building autumn embankments and roads, and the remaining 2,000 yuan for direct relief. Sihui County receives 20,000 yuan, with 15,000 yuan for building autumn embankments and roads, and the remaining 5,000 yuan for direct relief. Gaoming County receives 14,000 yuan, with 12,000 yuan for building embankments and roads, and 2,000 yuan for direct relief. Guangning County receives 14,000 yuan, with 11,000 yuan for repairing embankments and subsidizing house construction, and 2,000 yuan for direct relief. Sanshui County receives 5,000 yuan, with 4,000 yuan for building embankments and roads, and 1,000 yuan for direct relief. Qingyuan County receives 5,000 yuan, allocated in the same manner as Sanshui. Nanhai County receives 4,000 yuan, with 3,000 yuan for building embankments and roads, and 1,000 yuan for direct relief. Yingde, Yangshan, and Heshan counties each receive 2,500 yuan. Deqing, Huaxian, Yunan, Yunfu, Fengchuan, Wengyuan, and Qujiang counties each receive 1,500 yuan, allocated for repairing embankments, building roads, and direct relief. Furthermore, the Ren'ai Shantang charity recently noted that Shunde County is suffering from the decline of the silk industry, rural bankruptcy, and the impact of the floods, leaving the poor with no means of livelihood. Major surnames and clans in Daliang and Chencun have already begun providing affordable grain and distributing porridge. Concerned for the disaster victims, the Shantang also allocated 2,000 yuan in relief funds and sent representatives to the county to discuss relief distribution methods with the county government (July 31st).

Songjiang: Notorious Thieves Escape from Court Prison

Notorious thieves Li Yiming, from Anhui Province, and Jiang Biyu, from Funing, had been sentenced to imprisonment by the local court and were held in the detention center awaiting execution of their sentences. Both thieves had appealed the verdicts, but had not yet been transferred to Suzhou. Unexpectedly, today (the 6th, at 5:00 PM), the two thieves dug through the walls of their cell and escaped together. The guards discovered the escape, but the thieves had already vanished without a trace. The detention center has telegraphed all relevant law enforcement agencies, requesting their cooperation in the arrest.

Zhou Mian, the county accounting director, has been ordered to transfer to the provincial capital. His vacancy will be filled by Sun Jiaqi, the accounting director of Gaoyou, transferred by the Finance Department. After receiving the order, Sun arrived in Songjiang the day before yesterday and took office yesterday.

County Magistrate Inspects Seawall

The seawall in the Jinshanwei area of Songjiang has suffered some damage. After receiving the report, County Magistrate Jin scheduled a boat trip for today to inspect the seawall with the technical director Xu Mojia and others to design repairs.

Kunshan: Smuggling Opium Dealer Captured and Escaped En Route

Since Kunshan County began enforcing the opium ban, it has been very strict in arresting opium dealers. However, these people, driven by profit, are willing to break the law. A guest merchant named Zhu Haichun, who lived in the Likujie Street behind the county government, specialized in smuggling opium. Zhang Da, the director of the County Public Security Bureau, learned of this and, on the 5th at 11:00 PM, ordered Fang Zheng, the leader of the detective team, to lead four detectives to arrest him. Zhu was already asleep at the time and was easily captured. The police also found two large packages of cooked opium. The police handcuffed Zhu and took him to the bureau for processing. However, when they reached the Phoenix Bridge, the suspect took advantage of the police's inattention and escaped without a trace. The police urgently searched everywhere and fired shots to warn him, but were unable to recapture him. As a result, Zhu's wife was detained at the bureau pending further action. Today, detectives have been dispatched to various locations to strictly apprehend the suspect, but it is unknown whether they will be successful.

Newspaper Office Vandalized

The Kunshan Dan Bao newspaper, which has been published for only five months, has changed ownership twice due to financial difficulties. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, Jin Fangliu, the former editor-in-chief of the newspaper, along with Zou De, a staff member of the science laboratory, Chen Zheng, a teacher from a certain school, and two servants, went to the newspaper office to argue with the publisher, Lu Jiandan. Lu was not there at the time, so Jin and the others vandalized the office, tearing up various manuscripts and removing the sign at the entrance. After a while, Lu returned to the office and learned of what had happened. He immediately reported the incident to the County Public Security Bureau, who sent police to investigate. It is said that the incident was due to a dispute over investment funds, leading to this act of anger.

Suzhou: Suzhou-Kunshan Highway Scheduled to Open

After the completion of the Suzhou-Shanghai highway, it has been decided to open the Suzhou-Kunshan section for ticketed traffic on the 11th of this month. The route starts from Quanmen in Suzhou and passes through Qianwanli Bridge, Qimenwai, Guanli, Waikuatang, Weiting, Zhengyi, and ends at Men, with a total of eight stations. The vehicles used, four Ford trucks, have already been shipped from the Provincial Highway Administration yesterday (the 6th). They are smaller than the larger Mengtian trucks, with 15 passenger seats per vehicle. Shen Shaozeng has been appointed as the station manager of the Kunshan station. The opening of the entire highway will be implemented after consultation with the Shanghai Municipal Government, which should not be far off.

Suzhou-Wuxi Highway Planned for Construction

The Provincial Construction Department recently instructed the Wuxian and Wuxi counties to complete the construction of the Suzhou-Wuxi road within the year. The construction bureaus of both counties have already begun surveying and are preparing detailed plans and budgets to be submitted to the province for approval. Construction is expected to begin after the Mid-Autumn Festival. It is said that Wu will begin organizing the Suzhou-Wuxi Road Engineering Office, stationed in Changzhou and Zhenjiang, to oversee the construction.

Throwing Soil at Train Case Referred to Zhenjiang for Strict Handling

The case of throwing soil at a train on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, after the arrest of the main suspects Xue Songshan, Wang A'er, Liu Ziyang, and Chen Yinsheng (the owner of the Qingji soil shop, also known as Qian Qing), has attracted widespread attention. The suspects have now been sent to the county for transfer to the Zhenjiang Garrison Command for strict handling. Whether the driver and crew of the train were aware of the incident also needs to be investigated. Therefore, the County Anti-Opium Committee has sent a letter to the management of both railways, requesting them to investigate thoroughly.

Public Security Bureau Actively Kills Stray Dogs

The problem of capturing stray dogs in Suzhou has been reduced since the Public Security Bureau began actively killing them on the 1st of this month. To facilitate the registration of domestic dogs, the deadline for supplementary registration has been extended by ten days. At the same time, a religious philosophical society has launched an animal protection association, appealing to the authorities to slow down the capture. Amidst the dispute over whether human life or dog life is more important, an apprentice at a wonton shop in Dongzhong Market was bitten by a domestic dog. The stray dogs that have not been killed are still rampant, and even domestic dogs with registration tags around their necks are lying on the streets, barking at people. As of yesterday (the 6th), the preparatory committee of the animal protection association has decided to set up a shelter at Xiajin Bridge, build straw sheds, and discuss management methods. It has also submitted a request to the authorities to capture dogs alive and send them to the shelter for adoption. Meanwhile, the Public Security Bureau has decided that all registered domestic dogs must have their owners purchase and wear muzzles, otherwise they will still be captured and killed.

Wuxi: Silk Market Soars, Work Intensifies

Recently, the overseas silk market has seen a decrease in Japanese silk production, leading to higher silk prices. European and American foreign firms are increasingly ordering Chinese silk because of its soft texture and lower price. Silk factories in Shanghai are busy processing and reeling silk. More than thirty factories in Wuxi have started production, accounting for one-third of the total number of factories. Currently, 85-point Imenna silk can be sold for around 500 yuan, and 83-point old silk can also be sold for 470-480 yuan. Household silk is currently priced at 440 yuan, more than 100 yuan higher than when it was at its lowest. As a result, the price of dry cocoons has also risen, with the highest price being 180 yuan. In the past few days, Shanghai factories have come to Wuxi to purchase 780 bales of spring dry cocoons, priced at 180 to 165 yuan. The Wuxi Silk Factory Association held an extraordinary meeting yesterday to resolve the following: (1) Since August 1st, the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Bureau has canceled the freight cars attached to the early passenger trains, which greatly hinders the silk being sent to the Silk Inspection Bureau and delivered to foreign firms. The bureau will be asked to restore the original situation. (2) The Shanghai industry will be consulted to reduce silk sales commissions and ensure strict compliance. (3) There are inconsistencies in the wages and working hours of female workers in various factories. A uniform method should be established. It was decided that starting this month, the standard wage for silk reeling workers will be 42 cents, and those who were previously paid 30 cents will switch to full-time work starting from the 7th. The working hours will be uniformly set as starting work at 5:00 AM and stopping work at 6:30 PM, with a 15-minute break for breakfast and a one-hour break for lunch.

Meijing Township Police and Bandits Engage in Fierce Battle

The farmer brothers Qian Chunqiu and Chunhua from Shanglouxia Township, Meijing, in the tenth district of the county, recently received association funds, which attracted the attention of bandits. At 11:00 PM the night before last, six bandits suddenly arrived and broke into their house. Three bandits carried box cannons, two carried pistols, and the rest carried iron rods. They tied up the Chunqiu and Chunhua brothers, forcing them to reveal where the silver was hidden. They then robbed 13 silver dollars and over 20,000 copper coins, as well as gold jewelry and clothing, from the room of Chunqiu's mother, Zhou. As they were leaving, they encountered the son of their neighbor Zhang Baifu, who was outside with a flashlight. They tied up Zhang's son and broke into Zhang's house to loot it. At that time, Zhang Baifu took the opportunity to secretly report to the Duomenqiao Water Patrol Team. Team leader Cai led the team to rush to the scene. The bandits were alarmed and fired shots to warn them. The two sides clashed, fighting fiercely for more than ten minutes. The bandits took the opportunity to escape. At the time, it was dark and they could not be pursued. Yesterday, they reported the incident to the county for arrest. Also, at around 10:00 AM that day, a Xiyu class cargo ship in Huangnitou was robbed of over 100 silver dollars, clothes, and bedding by three bandits. Yesterday, they also came to the city to report the incident.

Changzhou: Education Department Sends Personnel to Handle the Transfer of Women's Normal School

Zhuang Minqiu, the principal of the Wuyi County Women's Normal School, has been approved to resign. The Education Department has appointed Xiao Shiguang to replace her. Principal Xiao has come to the school to take over, but former Principal Zhuang requires several thousand dollars to resolve matters she handled, and the opening date of school is approaching. The handover has not yet been completed. In order to quickly resolve the matter, County Magistrate Hou specially telegraphed the Education Department, requesting them to send personnel to Changzhou to handle the matter. Yesterday (the 5th), an order was received, appointing Wu Dezhang and Zhu Niancheng to come to Changzhou to investigate and handle the matter, and ordering the county to handle it jointly. The two representatives from the Education Department also arrived in Changzhou from Zhenjiang at around 5:00 PM and discussed everything with the new Principal Xiao Shiguang. This morning (the 6th), they went to the county to discuss the solution of the handover with County Magistrate Hou.

Yangzhou: Seized Opium and Drugs, Arrested Suspects

Xu Baolin, the owner of the Xu Yonghe Hotel in Jiangjiaqiao Street, Yangzhou City, is known to be honest and sincere. However, suddenly at around 3:00 PM today (the 5th), Zeng, a member of the County Anti-Opium Committee, sent five police officers, along with one person, to search the hotel. They arrested Xu Baolin and took him away. It is said that the person who came with the police officers was the informant who secretly reported to the Anti-Opium Committee that Xu Yonghe was privately selling opium and drugs. The committee sent police to search the address and seized packets of opium and dozens of packets of drugs upstairs. The evidence was conclusive and they were taken to the committee for disposal.

Section Chief Goes to Shaobo to督堤 Work

Yang Guoxiang, the section chief of the seventh district of Jiangdu, followed the instructions of County Magistrate Ma and rushed back to Shaobo yesterday (the 4th). He immediately summoned the heads of the relevant townships and towns along the Yundong Dike to discuss the method of recruiting workers to build the dike, planning to recruit 8,000 workers to collect 80,000 cubic meters of soil. Today (the 5th), Tang Jianzhong, the section chief of the second section of the County Government, and Shu Guohua, the director of the Construction Bureau, took the Fuyun ship at 11:00 AM to Shaobo to supervise the work, with an estimated completion date of five days before returning to the county.

Odd Flowers at Fa Hai Temple are Deer Onions

The Fa Hai Temple on the Slender West Lake in the northern suburbs of Yangzhou suddenly has stone luck, or some say it is Qionghua, and it is publicized in the city and suburbs, with viewers following each other. According to Tang Shou, the principal of a private school, after visiting, he told people that the flowers grow in the bamboo forest, about five or six plants growing together. The stems are tender green, the top opens into an umbrella-shaped flower, with bracts, the petals are six-lobed, silver-red, six stamens accompany the flower throat, and one pistil extends beyond the flower. After investigation, this flower belongs to the Lycoris family, with the species name of Deer Onion, resembling daffodils, also known as Summer Daffodil. The leaves grow in winter and wither in summer, the flowers and leaves do not meet, and the flower stem has bulbs like a ball, which is a perennial herb. It is a medicinal plant with poison, as recorded in the Secret Flower Compendium.

Pinghu: Car Overturns and Falls into River

Yesterday, a Jin surname farmer woman living in the Shengdi Temple in Hongshu Township was walking in Pangjia Village, south of Hongni Town. A Min Ping joint transport passenger car from the Highway Bureau was speeding towards her. Before she could avoid it, she was knocked down. At the same time, the car rushed into the sidewalk and overturned into the river. The people in the car were greatly frightened. Staff members rushed to the scene, lifted the car, and sent the injured people to the Zhapu Chengji Hospital for treatment. The car was Zhejiang No. 61305, and fortunately there was no major damage.

City Area Carelessly Burns Down Herbal Medicine Store

The Yilong in this county, due to the previous conflict with the Public Security Bureau, dragged the dragon to the Public Security Bureau and abandoned it, and many were destroyed by the police. Therefore, the Public Security Bureau canceled it, and it was finished without finishing. Therefore, when Zhang Peichen's house caught fire last month, except for the dragon in this ward, not a single dragon went to rescue. The day before yesterday, a hurricane raged, and yesterday the Baoyuantang Pharmacy in the city reported carelessness, the Chinese medicine room behind the building, with thick smoke everywhere, and the sound of gongs filled the city in a moment. However, all the wards did not send out dragons, and the neighbors were anxious, and they went to drag out the dragon in this ward to absorb water and extinguish the fire. Fortunately, it was during the day and it was extinguished soon. Now the people of the county are extremely worried about the lack of fire administration.

International Commercial Telegraph

— August 6th, Reuter's Special Commercial Report —

Gold and Silver

British Gold: London gold price fell one and a half pence today, to one hundred and forty shillings and nine and a half pence.

British Silver: The London silver market was quiet today, with prices unchanged. Spot remains at thirty pence one eight seven five, and futures at thirty pence two five. The United States bought, while India and China bought and then sold. The market closed steady.

American Silver: Mountly silver futures market opened with prices unchanged. As the United States continued to purchase in the London market, sellers asked for slightly higher prices.

Exchange Rates

British-American: The London foreign exchange market was stable this morning, with no significant fluctuations in the price of the pound sterling. The opening exchange rate between the British pound and the US dollar was four dollars, nine corners, five cents, eight seven five, the same as the last closing price between the US and Britain. It rose one eight seven five within an hour to four dollars, nine corners, six cents, zero six two five. After that, the change was minimal, and the afternoon price was four dollars, nine corners, five cents, nine three seven five.

British-French: The opening price rose one pound, to seventy-four francs seventy-six. It rose six pounds in the first hour, and continued to rise three pounds at noon, to seventy-four francs eighty-five. There were no changes afterwards.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: The New York cotton market remained sluggish and uninteresting. As foreigners made slight purchases, the price rose slightly, but merchants remained on the sidelines, waiting for developments in Washington.

American Wheat: The Chicago wheat market and Liverpool prices rose, and the report on wheat production was also unfavorable. The opening price rose about one point. The Canadian official report on the heavy losses caused by wheat rust was also a reason for the wheat price to look higher, but there were many arbitrageurs, and many closed out positions. The market price soon fell back. The opening price of miscellaneous grains rose slightly in the near term, but soon rebounded. The price difference between September and December futures was even greater.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market was stable today, with no particular highlights. At 1:00 PM, the price for October futures was six point one two, up two pounds.

New York Commodity Prices

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market also rose today due to the rise in the American market yesterday and the continued favorable harvest report. At 1:00 PM, the price for October futures rose one penny, to five shillings four pence six two five.

Rubber

London: The London rubber market was stable this morning. At noon, the trading price for October-December futures was five pence nine three seven five, the same as the last closing price.

New York: The New York rubber market opened several pounds higher and was quite stable because no one was selling.

Securities

New York: The New York stock market opened higher this morning. The average price of the Dow Jones 30 industrial stocks rose thirty pounds, to one two six point three six. However, not long after the opening, the market situation changed and became uneven, and the buying interest was limited to a few special votes. The price of General Motors shares was particularly firm because of the announcement of the favorable dividend yesterday. The shares of Montgomery Ward and other department stores rose slightly due to the improvement in wheat prices. Oil stocks were stable, road stocks fluctuated frequently, and public utility stocks eased slightly as some people took profits. The various prices are as follows:

Letter to the Editor

To the esteemed editor, having read Mr. Zhou Xuewen's letter in your newspaper on August 3, which mentions "the lingering heartache of the missionary Bu," I must clarify that the funeral arrangements were discussed and agreed upon by the board of directors of the Orphanage for Poor Children and the Jiazi War Disaster Memorial Association beforehand. It was agreed that the condolence money received would be split equally between the two parties. As a result, the Jiazi War Disaster Memorial Association received 621 yuan, which will be used to rebuild the memorial pavilion. I have not interfered in this matter in any way. There is no so-called heartache. Fearing that the outside world may misunderstand the facts, I hereby make this statement. Please accept this for your esteemed consideration, O great editor of the Shen Bao. Respectfully submitted, William Brewster, missionary.
