Spring and Autumn

Snippets

— (Ji Yu)

Between the poor and the rich, there is only a thin membrane of happiness. This membrane is very thin, and it can be easily torn and flow to the neighbor. Therefore, the rich should protect their membrane, and the poor should destroy their membrane.

Anyone's money should be spent in the right place. The so-called right place can determine a person's meanness and wastefulness. In other words, spending a penny in the wrong place is wasteful, and not willing to spend all the property in the most appropriate place is stingy. Conversely, when money should not be spent, we must save a penny, and when money should be spent, we can squander all our wealth.

Poor and miserable people are often prone to success in their careers, just like iron forged in a raging fire, the more solid it becomes.

Therefore, those who want to succeed should not dislike poverty and hardship, hoping that they can endure this poverty and hardship.

Strange Omens and Anecdotes

— Lin Yi Tan

Whenever someone has an unexpected misfortune, recalling the events before the misfortune, they feel that there were omens预先 warning them, but no one can guess or understand them beforehand. Only afterward do they suddenly realize. This can be regarded as an inexplicable problem worthy of study. The following story has this kind of characteristic.

A clansman of mine, rich in wealth, is a giant in the Fuzhou financial world. Once, in a famous poetry club in Fuzhou, he was reciting the third verse of a "branch-plucking poem" for the sounds "xiang" (相, appearance) and "xiang" (鄉, village). (Branch-plucking poems are very common in Fuzhou, because there are more people who love poetry.) This clansman of mine wrote a verse: "Thieves who look familiar should not be missed, prostitutes who seem like villagers are worth recognizing." This unspeakable verse is naturally "Yu Yuan" (榆元, a type of poetry mistake). But the strangeness lies in the verse, which is the peculiarity of the omen.

Two days later, he and his family took a car to the suburbs for a drive. When the car drove far from the city, it was dusk, and all around were wheat fields. Suddenly, four or five kidnappers rushed out, first firing shots into the sky, and then intercepting the car, kidnapping only him. In the bandit's lair, he learned that one of the kidnappers was his former employee whom he had dismissed. Because the employee knew he was rich, he specifically investigated his travels and carried out the kidnapping.

There was also a strange thing: when he arrived at the bandit's lair, there was already a woman there. This woman was none other than his lover, a quite famous girl in Fuzhou. Because she was quite famous, she was also kidnapped by the bandits. They suffered together in the bandit's lair, and their feelings naturally deepened a lot.

Later, he was redeemed, spending more than 20,000 yuan. After he came out, he told the strange story of the omen, which was widely circulated and caused a sensation in Fuzhou.

Ying Gu

— Chen Qiu Nong

In a very large wasteland at the intersection of Xing Road and Yongxing Road, there are many performers who perform various arts every day. There are Peking opera, circus, as well as various Tanhuang and one-man shows, comedies, two-man shows, storytelling, Yangzhou opera, Shaoxing opera, national martial arts troupes, magic, and so on. It is also like an open-air big world. Every day, there are many spectators, like a mountain of people. Generally, small businesses compete to set up stalls and do business here.

Ying Gu is a woman who performs martial arts and sings ditties. She also sings and performs skills here every day. There are more than ten male and female performers in her troupe. Because Ying Gu is the most beautiful, she is considered the pillar of the troupe. More than a dozen people rely on her beautiful voice and appearance to make a living.

This afternoon, various performances began at the same time. Ying Gu's venue also struck the opening gong and drum at the same time. Before long, the spectators had surrounded each venue. Every day, except for the circus venue, Ying Gu's venue is always the most popular.

At this time, Ying Gu had already started performing. Another female performer lay prone on a square table, with her feet pointing upwards. Ying Gu went up and sat cross-legged on the soles of those upward-facing feet, said a few opening remarks, and then began to sing the "Touching..." ditty, with the title "Touching Everything," from a set of erotic folk songs. The surrounding spectators stared at her blankly.

The "Touching Everything" song was almost finished. Several performers next to her were preparing to ask the surrounding spectators for money to provide dinner for more than a dozen companions. Suddenly, a policeman walked out of the crowd, stepped forward and called her down, and said, "This ditty is related to public morals. Take you to the bureau to pay a fine."

Although Ying Gu is a woman who knows martial arts, with at least seven or eight police officers' resistance, but in the end, she did not dare to offend him. As a result, she closed the venue and stopped singing.

That night, the stomachs of more than a dozen people were affected by this police officer. Some were making echoes, and some were launching sirens, making a commotion all night long.

Double Heaven of Summer Heat Avoidance

Little Western Heaven

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Seventeen: Do Not Ask About a Daughter's Difficulties or Hidden Pain, Compete to See a Noble Person's Face and Admire Lofty Conduct Together

Yueying frowned and said, "When Master Jia goes out, he even wants to lock the door. I said that if you lock me in the room, it's like you're afraid I'll run away, and if others see it, I'll be embarrassed. He thought for a while before letting me close the door and sit in the room. If a friend comes, just say he's gone and don't open the door. You've come, and you're a woman, so I dare to let you in. Please sit down, is there anything I can do for you?" As she spoke, she knew to pour a cup of tea and put it on the table for the guest. Seeing her sitting on the bed, Huanhua also sat next to her, took one of her hands into her arms, and gently stroked it, saying, "Sister, tell me the truth, are you really happy with this marriage?" Yueying suddenly looked at her, as if she didn't expect him to say this, and said, "Isn't that obvious? I'm not hungry anymore, and I have clothes to wear." Huanhua still held her hand, and paid more attention to her face. She felt that her face was tight, and she wasn't smiling, so she put her hand on her shoulder and said, "I'm lying, am I? I don't think you're very happy." Yueying lowered her head, looking at her own hands, but did not answer. Huanhua said, "See! What did I say? You're sad again, aren't you?" Yueying looked up at him again, and then whispered, "I don't have anything else to be sad about, it's just that I can't see my mother, and I can't see my grandmother." Huanhua said, "Master Jia won't let you go back, can't your family come to see you?" (283)

Records of the Lingering Fragrance

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shou Ou

"Fathers often have to say to their children with tears in their eyes: 'I have no choice but to hit you now, but I myself am more painful than if I were hit ten times; if I hit you ten times, it's like hitting myself a hundred times. Your pain is on your body, but my pain is in my heart!'" Now that I have punished this minister, who has stood in court for a long time, in this way, the pain I feel in my own heart is really no less than what he feels!"

"However, things are already like this, we must quickly find other things to do, so that we can drive away these troubles; otherwise, how can we forget this matter? But we really have to forget it, because we have too many courtiers, and how can no one commit crimes again in the future? If someone commits a crime, of course, they will inevitably be punished, and if we accumulate troubles one after another, wouldn't we accumulate too much? We people with bad health, how can we stand it? If we are angered to death, it might not be enough! But what's the use?"

From the Empress Dowager's two conversations above, it can be seen that she still has some ability to distinguish right from wrong; she also recognizes that the things done by the Governor of Guangdong were wrong, which shows that she is not completely unable to distinguish between black and white. According to my usual careful observation, she not only sees clearly what other people have done wrong, but she can also be aware of any mistakes she herself has made, and she never deliberately covers them up, and can always admit them very frankly; of course, she will never be punished for doing anything wrong, or go to apologize to others. (383)

Another Explanation of You and You

— Hong Yang

This "Spring and Autumn" is caused by the odd surname draft, the debate of "You" (尤) with a dot and "You" (尢) without a dot. Now the descendants of Duke You Wenjian of Wuxi are compiling their genealogy and are uniting with the You surname of Suzhou. In Duke You Wenjian's handwritten notes, it can be known that at that time, the You surname did have a dot, but the two large clans of the You surname in Suzhou, Liu Jiabang and Fenghuang Street, did not have a dot. Therefore, it can be distinguished that Wuxi is the You surname (尤), and Suzhou is the You surname (尢). Thus, there is the following research.

According to archaeologists, the You lineage of Suzhou is a descendant of Fang Xiaoru of the Ming Dynasty. When Emperor Chengzu of the Ming Dynasty executed Fang Xiaoru's ten clans, Fang Xiaoru had a young son who escaped the net of heaven and did not perish. He fled to Suzhou and changed his surname to Tian (田). The shape of the character Tian is square on all four sides. Changing the surname to Tian was actually using the shape of the character as the surname, without abandoning the memory of the Fang surname. Later, the surname was changed from Tian to You (尢). Therefore, the You surname lineage of Suzhou is a descendant of Fang Xiaoru. The surname was changed from Fang to Tian, and then from Tian to the You (尢) surname.

This kind of legend is somewhat illusory, but investigating the Suzhou You surname clan, there is a saying that they were surnamed Tian seven or eight generations ago, and then they were surnamed You without a dot. With this saying, it can be somewhat certain that the Suzhou You is a descendant of Fang Xiaoru who changed his surname. Perhaps the reason for removing the dot from the You surname was to distinguish it from the real You surname, which can also convince people. However, the reason for changing from Tian to You later cannot be verified.

Now the descendants of Duke You Wenjian of Wuxi are compiling their genealogy. Although the You surname of Suzhou is missing a dot, and there is a legend that the descendants of Fang Xiaoru changed from Tian to You, but since the surname has been changed to You, it is naturally closely related to the You surname. Otherwise, why not be surnamed Zhao, Qian, Sun, or Li, but must be surnamed You and remove a dot? Of course, it has a great relationship with the You surname. Uniting as one clan is certainly not impossible!

Whereabouts

Summer Night in Chao Mountain

— Wang Fang An

It is best to escape the summer heat in the mountains. Looking at the peaks of Kuanglu, Mogan, and Huangshan, where skirts and shoes gather in recent times, this saying is indeed correct. Two or three years ago, I stayed in Hangzhou. I always went to the lake to cool off in the hot summer, especially at night. Every time, I would not return home until late at night when the moon set and the stars thinned. Often in the light of the lamps and the moon, gazing at the center of the lake, and looking at the mountains on the lake from a distance, I would always feel leisurely and yearn for it. I regretted being burdened by official duties and not pursuing it deep into the mountains! Since retiring to my hometown, the humble door has been closed for a long time. Daily chores of rice and firewood have long ceased to be a source of pleasure. Recently, I have been suffering from the heat, and living at home in a cramped space makes me feel suffocated, so I have begun to think far away. Several times I planned to travel freely, but ultimately failed to fulfill my wish. Thinking about my hometown, how could there be no beautiful mountains and rivers? Therefore, on a certain day of the month, I went alone to Chao Mountain to visit the monk Miyin and stayed at Bao Ci Temple.

At that time, Chao Mountain was known for watching plum blossoms, and its reputation even surpassed Deng Wei and Lonely Island. However, there are many lush pines and green bamboos in the mountains, which are also suitable for cooling off in the summer. Compared to the scenery, plum blossom viewers may not be able to appreciate one or two of them. After the plum blossoms bloom in the mountains, tourists gradually become sparse. By the time of midsummer, there are few traces of people, which is especially suitable for quietness. Coming here from the hustle and bustle, I truly feel like I am in another world! I came alone, and only the monk Miyin was left alone at Bao Ci Temple. The temple servants were busy with farming and had all gone up the mountain to transplant rice seedlings. The mountains were silent, as if I were outside of the bustling world.

I entered the mountain in the early morning. The monk Miyin and I had a very good relationship, and we often traveled and lived together without restraint. We sat on futons in his meditation room and had pleasant conversations. The bitterness in our hearts was especially interesting. After eating, we had wild vegetables and bamboo shoots, purple eggplants and green beans, as well as the temple's carefully made vegetarian ham and smoked tofu skin, accompanied by homemade rose wine. Although I am not good at drinking, I finished two cups. Although I never eat heartily, I ate three bowls. The flavor of rural life was fully experienced in the temple's kitchen. At noon, cicadas chirped in the treetops, listening to the high-pitched songs that soared into the clouds, slightly breaking the silence. I did not dislike their annoyance, but if I were not in the mountains, I could not have this state of mind.

That evening, the pine wind rustled, like roaring waves, the heat dissipated, and coolness arose on the pillow. It was quite like being in a jade pavilion in the sky, where the cold was unbearable at the heights! I occasionally peeked out the window at the moon in the sky, which was like mercury pouring on the ground. I gazed at the Lion Peak in the distance, which was high and connected to the sky, and the Saddle Mountain on the back, which was like a beauty shrouded in smoke. The beauty of a summer night in Chao Mountain is truly difficult to describe with a colorful brush!

After entering the mountain, I stayed for three days and nights. During the day, I slept soundly by the south window, quietly inhaling the refreshing breeze, dreaming of a sweet dreamland, and listening to the sound of the flowing spring gurgling to my pillow, cleansing my worries. Every night, I would either invite one or two farmers to chat about farming under the bean trellis or melon rack, or I would accompany the monk to the Hangzhou Tangqi car road, cross the Bai Su Mountain Bridge, look down at the clear stream, scoop up the moon in the water, or even row a small boat, leisurely in the middle of the water, letting the gentle waves send me swaying. Moreover, there are many temples in the mountains. Because of my relationship with the monk, I was also well received everywhere. Therefore, I either climbed to Maming Temple to overlook the night market in Tangqi, or entered Huacheng Nunnery to rub the ancient traces of Zhao Songxue's well curb inscription, or sat in the ancient Guanyin Nunnery to listen to the pine waves, or went to Si Shui Nunnery to draw natural spring water to brew bitter tea. And there are many futons and scripture scrolls in Bao Ci Temple for me to pass the time. This scene, this situation, I wonder if those who are addicted to mountains and rivers, in this humid and hot season, also yearn for it?

Seventeen years ago, I also took my younger brother to escape the summer heat and live in the mountains. At that time, I stayed at Da Yuan Temple at the foot of Saddle Mountain. The monk Miyin was the abbot of the temple, so we were very happy. The temple was less than a mile away from Chao Mountain, while Bao Ci Temple was still in the wilderness, like Yi Guang going to Luo Luo when she was still poor. Thinking about it now, seventeen years have passed since I first went there. Changes in personnel are immeasurable, not to mention the feeling of the sea changing into mulberry fields?

Education News

National Children's Reading Material Exhibition to be Held for Ten Days Starting November 15th

The Third Congress of the National Children's Year Implementation Committee has amended and approved the "Measures for the National Children's Reading Material Exhibition" drafted by the Executive Committee. The amended measures are as follows: 1. The purpose of this committee is to improve children's reading materials. 2. This committee will exhibit children's reading materials in the following categories: (1) Current elementary school textbooks and various other children's reading materials published by domestic bookstores or individuals. (2) Elementary school textbooks and various other children's reading materials published by domestic bookstores or individuals in the past that are now outdated. (3) Children's reading materials compiled by domestic educational institutions. (4) Publications, charts, statistics, etc. on the research of children's reading materials by domestic elementary schools and institutions. (5) Excellent children's reading materials from foreign countries (Soviet Union, United States, Germany, England, France, Italy, Poland, Japan). 3. Collection of children's reading materials: (1) Children's reading materials published by domestic bookstores or individuals will be directly collected by the National Children's Year Implementation Committee from the bookstores and individuals. (2) Children's reading materials and research results compiled by educational institutions will be requested by the National Children's Year Implementation Committee to be selected and sent to the committee by the provincial and municipal education departments and bureaus. (3) Excellent foreign children's reading materials will be submitted by the National Children's Year Implementation Committee to the Ministry of Education, which will then forward them to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, instructing embassies abroad to collect the best children's reading materials from the educational institutions of their host countries, limited to ten to twenty copies. 4. The National Children's Year Implementation Committee will request the Ministry of Education to appoint personnel from the National Institute for Compilation and Translation to review textbooks, and will also hire children's education experts to form a children's reading material evaluation committee to evaluate the various children's reading materials on display, classify them into grades, and submit their opinions to the committee. 5. Four weeks after the closing of the exhibition, the National Children's Year Implementation Committee will complete the compilation of the evaluation opinions on children's reading materials and submit them to the Ministry of Education for record-keeping and public disclosure, so that the editing community knows what to improve, and users know what to choose. If any undesirable children's reading materials are discovered, the committee may also request the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Interior to order their prohibition. 6. The National Children's Year Implementation Committee will submit special excellent children's reading materials to the Ministry of Education for commendation. 7. All activities of this committee will be handled jointly by the National Children's Year Implementation Committee and the Ministry of Education upon request. 8. The expenses of this committee will be provided by the National Children's Year Implementation Committee. 9. The exhibition period of this committee is ten days, from December 15th to 25th, 1935. 10. Local Children's Year Implementation Committees do not need to hold similar exhibitions. If they do, the results of the evaluation should be sent to this committee for compilation and submission to the Ministry of Education for record-keeping. 11. The exhibits of this committee will not be returned. After the exhibition, they will be permanently preserved in institutions related to the study of children's education. 12. These measures will be implemented after deliberation and approval by the standing committee members of the National Children's Year Implementation Committee.

Instruction from the Ministry of Education: Improvements to Various Colleges and Universities in Tianjin

Based on inspection reports, the Ministry of Education issued instructions on the 6th to various public and private colleges and universities in Tianjin to make earnest improvements. The original instructions are excerpted separately below:

Beiyang Engineering College: An order to National Beiyang Engineering College states, in essence, "This college has previously been instructed by the Ministry to make improvements based on key points. Upon reviewing the report from the recent inspectors, it is found that the college has made considerable efforts in expanding equipment and conducting research over the past year, with particularly notable achievements in mechanical manufacturing research. However, the following points still require attention and implementation, and a report should be submitted for verification: 1. In terms of equipment, the mining machinery, ore dressing equipment, and the content of the fitter and planer workshops all need to be enriched. Alloy electric furnaces should be added as soon as possible. 2. In terms of teaching, a proper implementation plan for the practical work of mining and metallurgy students should be established, and the time for physical science demonstrations and experiments should be increased. 3. The college's mechanical manufacturing research is highly relevant to China's current needs, and the experimental expenses should be appropriately increased to facilitate this research work."

Hebei Provincial Women's Normal College: An order to Hebei Provincial Women's Normal College states, in essence, "This college has previously been instructed by the Ministry to make improvements based on key points. Upon reviewing the report from the recent inspectors, it is found that the college has generally paid attention to implementation over the past year. However, there has been no significant progress in the two areas of increasing the number of full-time teachers and raising the level of students. Therefore, continued efforts should be made to improve in accordance with the previous order. In addition, the equipment for food chemistry in the home economics specialization should also be added, and a practical program should be properly established to facilitate implementation. As for the college's request to change the physical education specialization back to a department, it is found that the college's preparations for physical education teachers have slightly improved in recent years. It is advisable to first focus on running the specialization seriously and pay attention to the universal training of all students in physical education. Expansion can be considered after achieving success. It is hereby ordered to comply and report."

Hebei Provincial Industrial College: An order to Hebei Provincial Industrial College states, in essence, "This college has previously been instructed by the Ministry to make improvements based on key points. Upon reviewing the report from the recent inspectors, it is found that the college has earnestly implemented the points raised in the Ministry's order, and there has been much progress in other areas as well. Despite financial difficulties, the college has been able to strive for the enrichment of equipment, and the school's simple and progressive academic atmosphere has become increasingly evident, which is commendable and gratifying. However, the teaching hours of full-time professors should still be reduced to allow them to devote more effort to manufacturing research work. The educational aspect is quite thorough, but attention should be paid to cultivating students' spirit of self-government and autonomy. It is hereby ordered to comply and adhere to it."

Tianjin Industrial and Commercial College: An order to Tianjin Industrial and Commercial College (private) states, in essence, "This college has followed the Ministry's key points for improvement and implemented them accordingly. According to the inspectors' report, some important instruments and machines have been added over the past year, and the allocation of funds is still in accordance with regulations. However, there are still points that need to be improved, which are listed below: 1. Teachers who are incompetent should be eliminated and replaced with excellent experts as full-time teachers. Part-time jobs and classes taken by faculty members outside the college should be strictly restricted. The president should not hold part-time positions outside the college. 2. Equipment for material testing and practical tools for various factories should be purchased as much as possible. The science museum should be built as soon as possible. 3. The college runs night classes without reporting them. The details of the operation should be submitted to the Ministry for approval. It is hereby ordered to comply and report."

A special notice was issued yesterday, which stated: "We have received Order No. 4836 from the General Private Education Department of the Ministry of Education. After reviewing the organization and curriculum of private schools, it is found that many of them do not comply with the provisions of educational laws and regulations. Most of their teachers also do not meet the qualifications for elementary school teachers, and they are often unaware of teaching and training methods. Therefore, they should be strictly banned. However, at a time when education is not yet widespread and timely, it does not hinder the enrollment scope of local elementary schools and can be allowed to exist. At the same time, the educational administrative authorities should take various measures to improve them, so as to assist in the promotion of compulsory education. In order to improve private schools and promote compulsory education, the bureau is hereby ordered to instruct the educational administrative authorities of the counties and cities under its jurisdiction to recruit local private school teachers during the summer vacation from this year onwards to hold private school training classes. The subjects should be taught with basic knowledge and teaching methods in Mandarin, arithmetic, and general knowledge, etc., according to the actual needs of the private school teachers. The lecture should focus on practical issues and practice, rather than merely lecturing on theory. After the lecture, an examination should be added as a basis for rewards. As for the specific measures for the private school teacher training class, the bureau should quickly draft them in detail according to local conditions and submit them to the Ministry for record. The private school teacher training book measures are now announced for public knowledge, and all private school teachers should submit reports to the schools in the district where they are located from the 10th to the 20th of this month, according to the form, and should not extend the deadline. This notice is hereby issued."

Lixin Accounting School: A Branch School of the Evening School Department is Added in the Nanshi District, Located at No. 25, Xuexi Street, Wenmiao, Ximen

The Lixin Accounting School at No. 190, Ningbo Road, in this city is affiliated with the Lixin Certified Public Accountants Office, which is headed by Dr. Pan Xushu. It has two departments: correspondence and evening school. The correspondence department enrolls students year-round, and students can enroll at any time. The evening school department enrolls students twice a year, in the spring and autumn semesters. This year's spring class has already ended, and the autumn class is scheduled to start on August 29th. The classes are divided into elementary and advanced levels. The elementary level includes five subjects: elementary bookkeeping, advanced bookkeeping, Chinese group, English group, and commercial arithmetic. It is specially prepared for beginners to study. The advanced level is divided into seven subjects: advanced accounting, bank accounting, company food accounting, government accounting, accounting mathematics, cost accounting, and auditing, for those who already have a considerable level to study further. In recent years, the social need for accounting talents has become increasingly widespread, resulting in a surge in the number of students applying to the school each semester. Due to the school's location, the number of students per semester could not exceed 340 or 350, so dozens of people who registered late were often unable to join. In the previous semester, in response to the demands of all parties, several classrooms were added to the Xinhua Bank on Jiangxi Road. This semester, in order to facilitate students residing in the Nanshi area, a branch school has been added at No. 15, Xuexi Street, Wenmiao Road, Ximen, Nanshi, to avoid the trouble of students traveling long distances in the evening. The registration office is still at No. 190, Ningbo Road. It is reported that since the enrollment began, the number of applicants has been very enthusiastic.

The Chinese Education Office of the Shanghai Municipal Council has recognized that the school is run seriously and has awarded the school 10 scholarship places. Students from poor families who have excellent academic performance can apply to the school. After approval, high school students will receive a subsidy of 40 national currency per year, and junior high school students will receive 30 yuan. The school is scheduled to hold new student exams on August 7th and 8th.

Pujiang Vocational Middle School: After Pujiang Primary School was taken over by Li Boqing, Wang Fengcai, Ma Lun, Geng Keming, Lei Zhen, and other members of the Jintan Shanghai Fellow Villagers Association Preparatory Committee, they made painstaking efforts, worked hard to prepare, spared no effort, and did their best to develop it. Although the scale of Pujiang Vocational Middle School and Primary School is rudimentary, the equipment can be said to be well-prepared, and they have hired Sheng Gong, Xu Lishiqing, and other gentlemen, as well as Gao Pa Lian, Li Yaqin, and other ladies, as teachers. Therefore, the number of students who have recently registered is very enthusiastic.

Wulun Women's Vocational School: The Wulun Women's Vocational School at No. 1555, Lafayette Road, French Concession, in this city, has been planned and operated by the principal, Zhu Lin, and is now adding equipment and striving to expand. More than 60 people were admitted in the first examination. The second examination is scheduled for the 20th of this month, and for the convenience of students from afar, they can take the exam at any time. Wulun Primary School and Kindergarten have also been added, and the number of students who have registered is very enthusiastic. It is also reported that the school is scheduled to open on the 26th of this month.

Private Shanghai Middle School: Private Shanghai Middle School and Shanghai Kindergarten have gardens and flowers, which are most suitable for students to rest. Starting this semester, 12 new high-rise buildings have been added to the south and are all in use. The student dormitories are all painted with pine lacquer, and in other aspects of food, a food inspection department has been organized to ensure that it is suitable for hygiene. Those who have registered in recent days have been very enthusiastic.

The Launch of the Jintan Children's Library

Chen Fusheng of the Jintan academic community in Shanghai is extremely enthusiastic about social undertakings in his hometown. He first created a children's hygiene team two years ago. Little Men (7)

— Original by Ms. Louisa May Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang (Zonghai)

When Little Ned brought the bottle over, his cheeks were red from exertion, so after Nat bravely took a dose, Mrs.裴 let him lick the spoon and used a piece of flannel to warmly wrap around Nat's neck.

〇〇〇〇〇〇〇〇〇〇〇〇

These preliminary treatments were not yet complete when suddenly, a bell rang, and a flurry of footsteps passed through the stairwell, indicating that it was dinnertime. Shy Nat trembled at the thought of meeting so many unfamiliar boys, but Mrs.裴 extended a hand to him, and Rob, with a protective air, said, "Don't be afraid; I'll look after you."

Twelve boys, six in each row, stood behind their chairs, eager to start eating immediately, and the tall youth playing the flute was trying to calm them down. However, no one sat down until Mrs. 装 was seated behind the teapot, and she pointed to Nat on her right, introducing him to everyone.

"This is our new boy, Bai Nai德. You can greet him after dinner. Be quiet, children, be quiet."

As she spoke, everyone stared at Nat before slipping into their seats, trying to be well-mannered, but the opposite happened. Mr. and Mrs. Pei did their best to ensure that the boys behaved well during meals, and they usually succeeded because their rules were simple and reasonable. The boys knew that the couple was helping them, seeking their happiness, and they tried their best to obey. However, at times, the hungry boys had a tendency that could only be restrained by force, especially on Saturday evenings after a half-day holiday.

Sports News

Our Davis Cup Player Xu Chengji Returned to Shanghai Yesterday and Will Perform in Shanghai for Two Days Before Returning to Java on the 15th

Our Davis Cup player Xu Chengji and his manager Mr. Carlson returned to Shanghai yesterday on the American ship President Jefferson. The ship docked at the Bailianjing pier in Pudong at 9:00 am. Many tennis enthusiasts from Shanghai, including Lin Baohua, went to welcome them. Mr. Xu went to his residence at 137 Seymour Road to rest. His remarks are recorded as follows:

Impressions of America: Mr. Xu stated that his trip to the United States to participate in the Davis Cup tennis tournament was primarily for observation, so he didn't mind losing. After participating, he deeply felt the progress made by European and American countries in tennis skills in recent years. The Chinese tennis community urgently needs to catch up. His first thought after returning from the Davis Cup was that the Chinese tennis community cannot cooperate. In ordinary times, they can compete with each other, but during international competitions, they cannot cooperate. The promotion of tennis is even more urgent because it is a very noble and relatively simple sport. Both men and women, young and old, can learn from each other with two or more people. It is very common in European and American countries, whether in cities or villages. In China, only a small number of cities have this sport, and remote areas do not even know what tennis is. In the future, he hopes that the tennis community and the entire nation will vigorously promote it.

Scheduled Return to the South: When asked about the domestic circles eagerly hoping that he could perform in Shanghai for a few days to help the victims of the Yangtze and Yellow River floods, Mr. Xu said that he was very willing to help the disaster victims, but he was afraid that his time was limited and could not perform too much. It is reported that Mr. Xu is scheduled to return to Java on the 15th. A friendly match will be held on Saturday and Sunday. Tennis fan Chen Qihao has scheduled a tea party for tomorrow afternoon at 4:00 pm.

Free Talk

Sex and Art

– Cheng Xuehong

Arishima Takeo said, "Love is what produces art." Indeed, the torrent of love beautifies the world. When people discover beauty, they create an idealized form of it as a symbol. The creation of art happens at this moment.

Historically, the germination of art originated from the cartoons, clothing, and tattoos of primitive peoples. According to Grooes, Australian aborigines carry a bag containing red, yellow, and white pigments when they go out. They proudly apply a few spots on their cheeks on ordinary days, and paint their bodies in various colors during wartime to intimidate the enemy. During festivals or victory celebrations, they apply colors all over their bodies to attract women. Red is suitable for both war and courtship, so it is the most valuable color. Therefore, there are tribes where people fight for weeks to obtain red pigment. Compared to women, men use more color; some tribes strictly prohibit unmarried women from applying color to their heads.

At Australian night dances, dancers often use white paint. In the Palti dance, both red and white are used. The Marrinyeri tribe decorates the bodies of the dead with bright red mineral earth. In short, the sole purpose of body painting in primitive times was to seek beauty.

A major drawback of using pigments is that they fade easily. Therefore, primitive tribes sought permanent art forms, creating aesthetic forms to increase their value.

Tattooing is the most common method. They pierce the skin with flints, shells, or other primitive knives to create patterns, then embed pigments underneath to make them last. In some Australian tribes, tattoos are mainly applied to the back, while in others they are applied to the wrists, chest, abdomen, and legs. This procedure is used on both sexes, but men's tattoos are often more extensive than women's. The styles of tattoos vary, including spots, curves, and straight lines. Sometimes the entire chest is covered with cuts (see "Natural History of Man" by Wood). The natives of the Torres Strait tattooed thick horseshoe-shaped scars on their shoulders, resembling military decorations; this is the most cruel primitive art.

The initial purpose of clothing was more decorative than practical. When Darwin saw a Fuegian native about to freeze to death and gave him a red garment, the native was overjoyed and tore it into strips, distributing them to his companions as decorations around their shivering legs, surprising Darwin. This is the same as the pursuit of beauty by modern women in the 20th century, who expose their chests and wear silk stockings even in the dead of winter.

The Eskimos in the Arctic also did not forget to decorate. They sewed colorful scraps of leather, teeth, bones, metal beads, copper bells, etc., onto their leather clothing. Women's clothing decorations are as complex as men's and include a loincloth (a dangling piece behind the back) that reaches the knees to distinguish them from men.

Civilization historians are dedicated to this fascinating work, explaining in plain scientific terms how great our cultural construction is for various states of civilized nations. They often consider the unevenness of this clothing and decoration to be an amusing example of the childish simplicity of those barbarians who cannot distinguish between the necessary and the unnecessary.

Since primitive people had considerable decoration on their bodies, they extended it to utensils. They painted colors on weapons and all daily stone tools and carved the beasts they longed to capture or the totems they jointly worshiped on the walls of caves to show their beauty.

Architecture originated from tombs. The oldest buildings in the world, the Egyptian pyramids, are tombs. The earliest chapels were shrines for the dead, where the living paid homage. Later, the tombs were gradually moved to nearby locations, but famous ancestors' tombs, such as Westminster Abbey, are still buried in the abbey. This simple chapel was the beginning of the temples that the Greeks built for Pallas Athene and the gods, and it was also the prototype of Gothic Cathedrals. In these temples, there were altars, which were sacred places for displaying the relics of the dead, their meaning similar to the original tombs.

Not only religious art must draw living sources from love to nourish its life, but other elements of creative art must also be combined with love. The beauty of rhythm and love are connected to produce dance, poetry, and music.

Primitive dance is the most direct, complete, and powerful expression of primitive aesthetic emotion. In dance, primitive people undoubtedly saw the most intense enjoyment of beauty that they could universally feel. That is to say, dance can grant sexual satisfaction. Hunting tribes usually have dances performed solely by men, while women only provide musical accompaniment. But there are also dances in which both men and women participate, which undoubtedly aim to arouse sexual desire.

Poetry is the verbal expression of internal or external phenomena in a form that achieves beauty for a certain aesthetic purpose. This definition includes subjective poetry, namely lyric poetry, which expresses internal phenomena - subjective emotions and ideas - and objective poetry, which expresses external phenomena - objective facts and events - in narrative and dramatic forms. In any case, its expression is solely for aesthetic purposes, meaning that the poet does not intend to stimulate behavior, but to appeal to emotions. Grey said, "Old Australians simply sing as a matter of course. They sing in anger, joy, and hunger. If they drink - unless they are so drunk that they lose consciousness - they sing even more."

Music, in its nature and influence among the arts, stands in an incomparable position, forming an independent art in itself. All other arts must be used for the purposes of life, while music is used entirely for the purpose of art. As Kubota Mantaro of Japan said, "A poet is like a child." In this sense, music can be called the purest art. Especially between music and poetry, although they have close connections on the surface, there exists a very deep internal contradiction. Poetry dominates the entire world of phenomena, while music itself can say, "My kingdom is not of this world."

The latent source of sexuality can nourish the artist's creative desire, and sometimes sexual love and art arise simultaneously. This is how the geniuses of the Romantic era were born. In these geniuses, imagination triumphed over reason, and sexual love and art simultaneously consumed them. Because the torrent of desire frequently surged, they were sensitive, passionate, devoted to fantasy, and without restraint. Their pain was also endless. They all walked extreme paths. Only by creating poetry, painting, music, and all philosophies of love can we follow them and express sympathy. At the same time, humanity is able to continue endlessly, and life is able to exist immortally, all thanks to this creative power.

"Art science must begin with the primitive art of primitive peoples." I believe this slogan of anthropologists.

Elegant Pursuits of Distinguished Men – Composing Poetry by the Stream

– Hu Kao

University Days (39)

– by Theodor Storm, translated by Chen Yin

I circled around her and went to the earth-field, where I waited for her. Soon I saw the flash of white clothes and the sound of the girl's light steps, and then she stood before me, still catching her breath. - Now I am again with her, alone together in the darkness of the summer night; but this is another kind of situation. I had not yet spoken to her when she took out a roll of paper from her bag; at that moment another flash of lightning showed that it was a letter, and the stamp and sealing wax on the letter were also visible. "This is from Christopher," said Nali, and she put the letter in my hand when I involuntarily reached out for it.

"From Christopher"! I shouted, "When did you receive this letter"?

"Today"! She replied softly.

"Then you still ran here"?

She didn't answer.

"Can I see this letter, Nali"?

"I was just about to ask you to read it."

I walked behind the house to a window with light. Li slowly followed me; I felt that her eyes did not leave me while I read the letter.

It was a long letter. Christopher explained why he had not written for so long. He had taken over his uncle's business; but his relationship with this business was still wavering, because everything depended on whether his cousin could marry a wealthy chimney sweep master: when a fellow villager who was a tailor came to visit him, he was already busy making new furniture for the bridal chamber, but the marriage suddenly changed; now everything was finally settled, his cousin had already married, and he would soon be able to obtain master qualifications in a foreign country; so now he invited her to go there, because he had no time to come here to pick her up. "As soon as I receive your reply," the last paragraph of the letter said, "I will immediately send the travel expenses; these travel expenses have already been raised and stored separately. The house is easy to find; there is a linden tree next to the green wooden bench in front of the door, just like in your parents' house; the house that I arranged for this young master and mistress is completely shaded by this linden tree!"

I folded the letter and handed it back to her. But Nali shook her head. "Please write a letter to him, Mr. Fei Li"! she said, two tears flowing down her cheeks; she added in a low voice: "His kindness is very touching."

"So you don't want to go yourself"? I asked.

She looked at me with a pleading, desperate look that made me regret that I should not have asked her this question.

"Nali," I said, "can someone help you"?

Our Levee Broke (Part 2)

– Hei Ying

"I don't think it's stable like this," said a young man.

"Not stable? Who is talking"! Old Ba, who had his leg broken by a waterwheel last year, stopped his hoe and shouted.

"I'm saying it." The young man stood up straight and faced him. "Look at this, it's just dug up and not plastered. Why do we still need to pay for levee repairs? Where did that money go? Our work is for nothing"!

"Yes, let's ask Mr. Huang"!

"That guy is farting," Old Ba rushed forward and shouted.

"What's wrong, Old Ba"? The young man went up to him, "You are also a commoner, and your wife and children are also behind the levee; if the levee is unstable and breaks, won't you suffer losses"?

"You speak so nicely! Then isn't Mr. Huang's house also behind the levee? Does he hope that the water will flood his big house? His property..."

"His property is in Shanghai, you know"? The young man replied calmly, smiling. "Don't you remember, he always runs away to escape from the bad rumors! Who is suffering in the end? Who is it"!

"That's right! Who is it"! I said sarcastically to Old Ba, whose face was turning green, feeling much more relieved.

The engineer rushed up and shouted. We all stopped working together and asked him to make the levee stronger. He went back to Mr. Huang to discuss; afterwards, armed soldiers specially sent down from the county were stationed to monitor everyone...

"The levee was indeed not repaired very strongly," the storyteller continued, and gradually got to the point, using gestures to help his expression. In the summer, it rained for half a month, and the upstream of the river rushed the water downstream. We inspected the levee bank, and heavens, it had reached a very critical state. Mr. Huang, he didn't care how anxious you were, he said he was writing a memorial to the superiors, waiting for the relief funds to be sent - but two days later he secretly slipped away to the county town and took the money"!

"Is it really so hateful"? Someone asked angrily.

"How could it not be true, afterwards Huang's family workers all followed him." He also expressed indignation. "I went back home just scratching my head, not knowing what to do with my wife. My sixty-year-old mother was sick in bed, if our levee broke, it would be really - one night, the night was so quiet that there was not a sound, and the rain cleared up; but lying in bed I could not sleep all night, my heart was jumping like crazy. Someone was watching the levee; but I seemed to hear the distant sound of a bell ringing several times, and I suddenly got up, scaring her pale. "There is no gong sound: there is no sound at all, you sleep quietly." But how could I fall asleep."

"Then what happened to your levee in the end"?

"It broke - in the middle of the night there was indeed a sad and urgent gong sound warning that the water had broken through the levee and was surging towards the village. People's voices became noisy, mixed with the cries of children, and the whole village was plunged into extreme terror. My wife and I quickly got up to help my mother, and also had to carry a large bag on our backs, and ran out in one breath. There were torches everywhere outside, and countless figures moving south. We struggled out of danger like this…"

"What about your mother"?

"She died on the road." He sighed and said. "Think about it, an old woman of sixty, who was already sick in bed, was forced to move by the water, and worried about her home being flooded, how could she not… not…"

A tear of remembrance for his home and mother dripped down, and the storyteller stopped speaking. He had struggled to escape here to find his cousin; but his cousin was a worker in a yarn factory, and a thatched hut cost fourteen yuan to rent - how could he maintain their lives with a salary that might be discounted? So he held his heavy head in his hands, sitting silently on the hot summer street, clenching his teeth, thinking of the fact that the levee broke, he could only sigh.

A List of One Hundred Drum Songs by Zhang

– Zhao Jingshen

Recently I saw the "Bibliography Studies" Vol. 4, No. 4 of the Japan Bibliographical Society, which contains a "List of Old Manuscript Drum Songs in My Collection" by Nagasawa Norihito, which lists 53 manuscript volumes of drum songs initially published by Baibenzhangtang (百本張堂). All of them were recorded in the "Baibenzhang Bibliography" (百本張書目). Baibenzhang was established during the Qianlong period, and this initial bibliography represents the drum songs popular during the Qianlong era. Many of them are now difficult to find. At least, some of the following species are not very popular; or to be more accurate, I have never seen them personally:

One Hundred Mountain Names, One Hundred Bird Names, One Hundred Black, Tenfold Grace, Mengzheng Hurrying for斋, Mengzheng Offering Sacrifices to the Stove, Thirteen Months of Ancient People's Names, Twelve Months of Ancient People's Names, Continuous Promotion of Three Ranks (two volumes), Liu Skilled Doctor Visiting the Sick, Door Gods Zao Wang Suing Merits, Mulian Monk Saving His Mother, Opera Troupe Names, Nine-Nine Chart of Ancient People's Names, Fisherman's Profit, The Most Joyful Spring Scenery, Exhortation to the World, Little Boy Hoeing the Ground, Two Eight Beauties, "A Floating Cloud Covers the Sky", First-Rank Official at Court, Fifteen Teardowns, Clever Little Girl, Confused Ancient People's Names, March Peach Blossoms Ten Landings, Encountering a Monk, Ten to One Hundred Watching Flowers, Begonia Blooming, Mother-in-law and Sister-in-law Offering Incense, June Three伏, Eight Difficulties, 彩樓配

The above 24 books obviously have a characteristic, that is, they rarely use historical subjects. Only "Mengzheng Hurrying for齋", "Mengzheng Offering Sacrifices to the Stove", "Mulian Monk Saving His Mother", "彩樓配", and "Liu Skilled Doctor Visiting the Sick" are based on old folk stories. This is very different from the drum songs that were popular after the Guangxu period of the Qing Dynasty, such as "Three Kingdoms", "Water Margin", and "Dream of the Red Chamber". Perhaps at that time, drum songs had not yet occupied the stage, but were just "walking the streets" and singing what was later called "civilized little tunes". The remaining 19 books still have lead-printed editions circulating, which are listed below, with annotations of the books they are found in and their publishing houses:

The following is from "Civilized Drum Song Lyrics", published by Beiping Zhonghua Printing Bureau, a total of 25 volumes. Each book is noted below the title:

(1) Luo Cheng Divining Fortunes (Vol. 8) (2) Luo Cheng Entrusting Dreams (Vol. 17)

(3) Changban Slope Two Volumes (Vol. 15) (4) Ten Loves Exaggerating Husband (Vol. 5)

(5) The Grand Assembly (Vol. 4) (6) Bao Gong Exaggerating Mulberry (Vol. 5)

(7) Han Xin Asking About Luck (Vol. 5, but titled "Han Xin Divining Fortunes")

(8) Eight Immortals (Vol. 12, but titled Eight Immortals Celebrating Longevity, not sure if it is).

The Grand Assembly and Ten Loves Exaggerating Husband also have small thin volumes published by Beiping Baowentang. The following are all from Baowentang edition:

(9) One Hundred Flower Names (no "儿" character) (10) One Hundred Insect Names (no "儿" character)

(11) Green Vegetable Names (no "儿" character) (12) Wine, Sex, Money, and Qi

(13) To Pick Up Inverted Reversal (14) Distant View of Azure Mountains One Stone

(15) First and Fifteenth Temple Gate Open (16) 蝍蟟 Divining Fortunes

(17) Beauty Playing with Parrot

A brief explanation is needed for the last five volumes. 蝍燎 Divining Fortunes is written as Grasshopper Divining Fate, One to Pick Up Inverted Reversal is written as Ten-Character Inverted Curtain, and Beauty Playing with Parrot is written as Parrot Matching Poems, not knowing if they are the same or different. "Distant View of Azure Mountains One Stone" is the first line of "Dislike the Poor and Love the Rich" (岔曲), and "First and Fifteenth Temple Gate Open" is the first line of "Prostitute Suing".

I hope this short article can be of some use for the exploration of the historical development of drum songs.

Local Supplement of Shen Bao

Casual Talks

Various Suicides

— Jia Wei

The growing trend of suicide did not begin today. Whether it's solitary, in pairs, entire families, or in groups; and the methods include self-slaughter, poisoning, drowning, jumping from buildings… and so on, all are directly and vividly annihilating one's own life, destroying one's survival functions. This is such a cruel and inhumane thing.

Therefore, from the very beginning of suicide, it has attracted the attention of society. Great arguments, brilliant insights, admonitions, prevention methods – everyone has been discussing them enthusiastically. Moreover, according to reports, "In recent years, the social economy has been depleted, unemployment is increasing daily, and suicide incidents occur daily… Finding ways to prevent this is truly essential. The Municipal Public Security Bureau, in light of this, has specially instructed the department to create cautionary illustrations depicting the pain of suicide, producing dozens of large-format pieces to be posted throughout the city in public places on roads, lanes, ports, wharves, riverbanks, and bridges in prominent locations, in order to warn those citizens who are momentarily pessimistic and contemplating suicide." After this, we believe that under such startling and "Turn Back is the Shore"-style large-format illustrations, "perhaps" the rate of fifty-four suicide incidents every half-month can be significantly reduced. However, what the eventual effect will be remains to be proven by the facts.

However, the so-called "suicide," generally speaking, only refers to the active aspect – directly destroying one's survival functions; indirectly shocking and causing people to avert their eyes. However, in addition to this, there are many other kinds of "suicide" methods, but they are not as likely to attract attention. This method can be called "passive suicide" and "chronic suicide."

The "philosophy of life" of "doing the work of one day like a monk striking the bell for one day" is very common in today's society. Moreover, there are even more people who embrace the "art of living" of sitting in "bitter meditation," drinking "clear tea," and "talking about ghosts." In this, they appear "pure," "elegant," to the point of resembling monks and nuns who have seen through the "red dust" and entered the "empty gate." However, strictly speaking, under this state of "getting by," they are waiting for the arrival of the final day of fate, which is also suicide.

As for ordinary young people, entering society, encountering cruel reality, and failing, becoming disappointed, and then discouraged, feeling sad, and becoming decadent... although they may not "immediately harbor thoughts of厌世," they will nevertheless become mentally disordered and abnormal. This is also suicide. Some live their lives in sadness and isolation, others enter places of decadent pleasure, indulging in paper and gold, to squander their youth and destroy their lives. The so-called "pessimistic literature," or "happy literature," and even "fatalism," can all be categorized as a type of suicide.

As for the larger picture, even more so when the nation's difficulties are imminent, those who sing loudly about "dancing to save the nation" with "entertainment not forgetting to save the nation" can also be said to be performers in this category.

Moreover, the madhouses are becoming overcrowded; eight or nine out of ten young people are sallow and emaciated, suffering from neurasthenia, and even lung disease stage ×, can it not be said that there is a direct relationship with this?

However, this is not accidental either. In today's bleak and desolate society, only the performance of "chronic suicide" or "passive suicide" is cultivated. In the realm of "active suicide," there are now "passive prevention methods" to "remedy" it. It is not known what "method" will be used to save those who are engaging in "passive suicide."

Summer Night at the Bay

— Yi

The thermometer has risen to over ninety degrees, and the city everywhere seems like a huge furnace spewing out hot and stuffy air. The sun seems to be stagnant all day, baking the earth. There is not a single breeze in the sky, and the white clouds are motionless, lingering on the edge of the sky. Under such hot weather, the asphalt on the road is melting, sending out white smoke. The leaves are sleeping, lifeless. A pedestrian walks by, drenched in sweat like a drowned chicken. Even dogs are lying tired under the shade of trees, stretching out their tongues, their bellies constantly rising and falling as they pant.

Indoors, the walls are hot, and the floors and everything else are emitting hot air. People living inside are dripping oil, as if ducks were put in an oven to roast. Humans who value politeness and have a sense of shame, men and women, in such weather, seem to have forgotten politeness and shame, shedding the nature of clothed animals. Everyone is baring their chest and back, exposing their arms and legs. If society were completely free, everyone would be happy to return to nature. The thin and short fabrics covering the flesh all feel as if they are carrying a thousand pounds of weight.

The island port, with mountains and water, although not as hot as the northern cities in summer, the long duration of the hot weather makes people feel depressed and miserable, just as the long duration of winter in the north makes people feel the terrible cold. Therefore, the people living in such a hot island city, except for a group who fight against heat and cold year-round for a living, everyone is seeking all kinds of comfortable, cool, and relief from the stuffy lifestyle in such steamy time.

People with leisure are clever and happy. During the day, although the heat makes them pant and sweat, they have already embarked on the path of happiness when the sun sets in the west and the western sky is still illuminated by a red glow.

The deep blue bay, the water is quietly still, without a single wave. Occasionally, a steamboat enters the port, the waves trailing from the stern of the ship, glowing in the light of the red clouds, are like pulling a scarlet golden chain. The water, heated by the sun, gradually cools down; a slight sea breeze blows from afar, like the goddess of liberty breaking the shackles for people, making people comfortable and intoxicated.

Countless small steam boats and sculling boats surrounding the Queen's Pier, each carrying young women and men, are sailing towards the vast bay. The city seems to be a bin for these people, group after group being spit out from all directions to the pier, and then carried onto the sea by small boats. Waves of perfume and laughter drift across the entire bay.

On the sea liner, it is also beginning to liven up. The joy of men and the smiles of women, which are not seen during the day, are overflowing everywhere at this time. The thick sound of the engine seems unable to break their whispers. All feelings of love seem to have been suppressed by the day's misery and are now being poured out endlessly under this great nature.

The stars in the sky twinkle, as if they feel the misery of the day like people and shine brighter in the night sky. The line of long snakes on the island city, the buildings circling around the mountainside, are flashing with colorful lights everywhere. In the shadows of the lights, people are living a short, happy night life, just like the people at sea. The dark sea surface is also illuminated by the scattered lights in the small boats.

Page 20

The city, the southern city on a summer night, is a happy, bright, and extraordinary land of joy for people. Everything in the world belongs to them.

Loan Shark Boss

— Ke Ming

—Contemporary Biographical Sketches

At dusk, because of the heat, everyone moves their dinner outside to eat. Thus, under this dim sky, in this hot air (filled with the smell of sweat, the clamor of conversations, and the crying of children), the small alley suddenly shakes off the fatigue of the day and reveals another noisy expression! People who work in factories, run errands in shops, do small business on the bustling streets, after a day's labor, all rely on this time, before putting their tired bodies on narrow and bedbug-infested beds, to chat idly, talk about serious matters of life, and discuss the obscene stories that unfold in the city every day, while nodding greetings to neighbors, amidst the noise of women and children, and also talk about "national affairs" and people's "private matters," laughing for a while, and sighing like rain – in this way, they temporarily pass a hard day, and at the same time, prepare to exchange essential labor for the life of the next day.

Just then, at the narrow entrance of the alley, came a tall man, wearing a "xiangyunsha" gown inside out, with the buttons undone; seeing this, most of the people in the alley (all those people whose income earned by labor is not enough to support their families and who must use the terrifying "loan shark money" to "supplement" it) were shocked, and suddenly remembered that today is the end of the month, yes, clearly, it is the end of the month, isn't this the "loan shark boss" coming to collect interest?

The "loan shark boss," straddling his huge body into the entrance of the alley, nodded vaguely to everyone; then, using his eyes, he called the names of his "debtors" in this alley one by one, while reaching into the pocket of his "xiangyunsha" gown, and pulling out a small, dirty, old-fashioned wallet: "It's time to collect the interest."

In this alley, there are quite a few families who, because the money they earn is not enough to "cover expenses," borrow "loan shark money" from the "loan shark boss," ranging from three or five yuan to twenty or thirty yuan (at a monthly interest rate of six and a half percent). They borrow because their daily money is not enough, and they are forced to take this "poisonous road." If they have to extract a portion of their already insufficient income every month to pay such heavy interest, of course it is not a very easy thing! Because of this, people feel a heavy weight in their hearts, like a large stone falling, every time they see the "loan shark boss" at the end of the month, and the "loan shark boss" knows very well that collecting this amount of interest every month is not an easy task, and he has to spend some words, cause some trouble, and finally, even resort to some small "tricks"!

Yes, "the world is bad, and people's hearts are not as good as before" (the loan shark boss sometimes sighs like that)! Greedy for a little interest, risking a large capital, this business of lending money is really not easy to do. If you don't have "tricks," if things go wrong, not only will you not get the interest, but even your "capital" will be lost, "these people are not good people! If I don't have some tricks, hum…"

Indeed, times are difficult, and people cannot repay the interest, that is the reality; but the loan shark boss's "tricks" are also the reality. He has his "old man," his brothers in the "gang," and also his subordinates; moreover, his "tricks" are known to the residents in this area.

Because of this, when the loan shark boss walked into the entrance of this alley, people remembered that it was the end of the month, and also remembered fear and sorrow; therefore, they had to take out the money for tomorrow's rice, some even took off their gowns to pawn them, some requested a day or two of grace because they really couldn't come up with "cash" at the moment, and some pleaded about their miserable circumstances, knowing full well that they would not be pitied – talking, scolding, cursing, explaining, pestering, all kinds of unpleasant tones mixed together, along with the boss's loud scolding, filled this small alley, and also filled the hearts of the people who were tossed and turned under the iron hands of usury, like sandbags at the mouth of a trench, and gravel stagnant at the bottom of the water.

Then, the boss frowned, scolding angrily, while counting the interest money that people "handed over," and stamped each one on the wallet with a red stamp, and then, without any slack, he turned to another group of people to confirm the exact date of payment.

"You say it, you say it! What day will you take it out, if you don't pay, it doesn't matter if you explain it; I, the boss, have been doing this business for more than a year or two! You can play tricks, but I also have my tricks! I… hum…"

Pressing and pressing, after getting a reply, he swayed out of the alley, turned a corner, and his huge figure disappeared.

However, people felt as if the loan shark boss's heavy footsteps were stepping on them. Day after day, he lives like that…

Peddler

— Shi Ying

Carrying a load on his shoulders, he walks from the main street to the small alleys, from the market towns to the villages. Every day, he drags his tired shadow and raises his dry voice, hawking the sundries in his load. —This load is the burden of life, bending his shoulders. The summer afternoon sun, like a fiery umbrella, covers the green fields. The yellow dog under the shade of the tree is also panting, sticking out its tongue. He carries his load, dripping with sweat, walking on that rugged village path. Seeing black-tiled houses and gray-white earthen walls in the mulberry forest embracing in front, he knows it is another village. Perhaps he can find customers there. The bell in his hand rings, shouting in a hoarse voice like a dull knife cutting things: "Foreign goods… Anyone want foreign goods? —Foreign socks, towels, soap, printed cloth. Anyone want…" Walking into that village, the first to welcome him is the mad barking of mangy dogs. The men may have all gone to the fields to work, and the old and young women cannot stand the dampness and heat in the house, so they sit on the square in front of the house; a tattered mat is spread on the ground, letting the children roll and sleep on the tattered mat, while they do their work in their hands. The ringing of the bell, the barking of the dogs, and the tempting call for customers naturally arouse their attention. Their eyes all look at the peddler. He carries a pair of small cabinets, and through the glass doors, you can see the things inside. Really, snow-white towels, pink and tender yellow foreign socks, colorful gauze, clever and cute miscellaneous items, soap, buttons, needles, and threads, everything is there. He is simply carrying a beautiful department store. All those things are what they yearn for on weekdays; they also know that the things on the load are cheaper than in the store, and it is easier to bargain. Flames of envy flicker in their eyes, but when they think of money, they think of how yesterday the men went to town, spent three-tenths of the interest, and begged earnestly to borrow five yuan, only to buy the fertilizer needed for cultivation now. They can only let their eyes be greedy.

The peddler is also clever. He cannot allow himself to have driven so many roads under the poisonous sun, but not sell a penny's worth of goods to go back. He rests his load under an old elm tree, taking off his old straw hat from his head and fanning his sweat and dust-covered face. But he calls out to them: "Auntie, want some good… Girl, this beautiful…" The young women all put down the work in their hands and gathered in front of his load, flipping through this and looking at that. Their voices are as jumbled as fried broad beans, asking the prices of everything, making it impossible for him to answer. Their bargaining mouths are even more sharp, as if they want him to give them away for free to be satisfied; difficult life, lack of money, they really want to see four words from a penny. As a result, the things in the cabinet were turned into a mess by them, and the transaction, only an old lady, spent two copper coins to buy a pack of needles. Those women, although envied around him, always reluctant to money. He was also not happy, because now such years see, whether to the town of that alley, the countryside of that village, all like this. From the morning to pick up the burden to go out, all day in doubt, today can be sold to a copper plate. But regardless of whether it is sold or not, he will have to live, he will eventually have to carry the burden of life to run around, he will eventually have to endure the suffering of life. Now the moment of rest in the shade of the small village tree is when he is the only happiness. So he asked a woman for a cup of cold tea, wiped the sweat and dust from his face with the corner of his clothes, and chatted with them. Naturally, the result of the conversation, everyone is sighing this year's children. …

The sun is about to set, and his day's run, a shoulder of heavy burden, has made him exhausted. But the load is still full and heavy, just like when he went out in the morning. He tenderly shook the bell in his hand, anyway, at this time there is no business to do. On the desolate village path, under the dim sunset, he returned to the town step by step, calculating a day's business, he can only bite his lips, but called dry throat, can not issue a sound. To the Buyun Bridge, it is already the market end, the lights of the town are sparsely decorated with dusk. He put down the burden, rested on the bridge railing for a while, and temporarily enjoyed the evening wind on the river. He thought of the dark home, maybe there is no light yet.

Opening "Begging for Help"

Tears fall before I can speak. The suffering of the disaster area is endless. I advise the good folks of the blessed land, don't dislike the nagging, listen to me. I dare not be envious and jealous. I just ask everyone to show sympathy. You live in peace in high halls and mansions. Who knows, there is endless suffering in the thatched huts. You wear fur coats and hats and still complain about the cold. Alas, barefoot and bareheaded are the miserable people. You have fish and meat for three meals a day. Alas, tree bark and grass roots are used as snacks. You have the joy of parents and children. Alas, flesh and blood separation, nowhere to find. You, the blessed people enjoy the blessings in the blessed land. We are born out of time as disaster victims. You know the rabbit died and the fox was sad. It hurts the most when things hurt their kind. Saving a life is a small feat. It is not a light crime to stand idly by. I beg you to generously donate money. I beg you to save clothes and food and do good deeds. I beg you to think about it yourself. I beg you not to take the lives of your compatriots lightly. I beg you, don't let your heart be as hard as iron. I beg you, show compassion and express sympathy. Alas, my stomach is hungry and my body is cold. Alas, I am dying in the disaster. Alas, I cried out for help and no one responded. Alas, I can't survive the imminent crisis. shout a sound. Good folks. Cry out a sound. Good sir. Saving a life is like putting out a fire. It should not be seen to die without saving. I think I am. My voice is tired and my throat is light. When I want to shout again, there is no sound. Help, help, teach me quickly.

MOVIE NEWS

"INSTANT LOVE" PREMIERES

Shi Benqu Laisai, the hero of "Twenty Thousand Years in Prison" and "Heaven Collapses and Earth Cracks," now co-stars for the first time with Wendi Palichu, a beautiful rising British starlet, in a so-called streamlined romance portraying 1935. They engage in numerous amorous and playful adventures in an extremely tiny world that barely accommodates you and me. As for the humorous insertions, the elegant scenery, the ingenious structure, and the lively and vivid sentiments, those are mere trifles in comparison to the rest of the film. This is truly an excellent and refreshing treat for young people immersed in the intoxication of love, and it is now being shown at the "Nanjing" cinema. The two leads of the film are on the left.

MAGNIFICENT MICROPHONE BROADCAST

Cheng Bu Gao's audio masterpiece "Night Blooming Jasmine," Hu Die's first work after returning to China (two-thirds of it was filmed before she went abroad), is said to be nearing completion. This is a sound film worthy of attention.

Xu Lai went to the Sports Garden yesterday to swim and was photographed extensively by Zhang Jinde, Chen Jiazhen, and others. The photos taken by Zhang Jinde will all be published in "Star Bi-Monthly."

In addition to working hard on filming "The Big Family," Zhang Shichuan is preparing his new work "Peach Blossoms After the Disaster."

Long Jianong, Wang Weixin, Wang Shizhen, and others practice tennis in the sun every morning, not stopping until noon. It is said that they are working so hard to prepare to organize a tennis team.

Since Gu Lanjun was praised by the Guanshengyuan Farm as the "Goldfish Beauty," the "Goldfish Paradise" has now invited her to perform the opening ceremony on the 6th (Sunday). Her elegant title of "Goldfish Beauty" is truly well-deserved.

CHINA ODDS AND ENDS

The "Water Country Spring and Autumn" Kaifeng location shooting team originally planned to return to Shanghai around the 5th of this month, but according to a telegram, there have been torrential rains in the area for days, so they fear they will have to wait a few more days.

The China Film Studio colleagues remaining in Shanghai invariably raise film technology questions for discussion after dinner every night, and they change the topic every night, aiming to use their spare time to make improvements in film technology. The clerk Kang Jingqiu records everything for future reference.

"Water Country Spring and Autumn" will include several songs to enhance the power of the drama.

China Film Studio cameraman Shi Shipan has now completed a labor drama script with workers' lives as the background.

China Film Studio colleagues will organize an amateur club to solve the problem of leisure activities.

Ms. Yan Qun, the Mandarin professor at China Film Studio, is not only a good singer but also a good dancer.

It is expected that Zhao Zhenni's healthy and beautiful posture in "Water Country Spring and Autumn" will break the general audience's psychology of worshiping weak female stars in recent years.

INTRODUCING "LITTLE ANGEL"

"Movies are good educational tools," is a universally recognized truth by leaders from all walks of life in the country, and Mr. Chen Guofu, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, is the strongest advocate among them.

Mr. Chen has continuously promoted this aspect, and the development of educational film undertakings in Zhenjiang is a clear proof of this.

In the past, Mr. Chen has compiled various film scripts for various companies to produce. Recently, in order to gather more ideas, he has openly solicited scripts.

Among the scripts solicited by the Jiangsu Provincial Government, "Angel" was selected as the first-place winner.

Using this winning script, and after extremely careful deliberation, the "Little Angel" of today was successfully created.

Because of the special achievements of Lianhua Film Company in the Chinese film industry, the Provincial Government handed this script over to Lianhua to produce.

With Wang Renmei, Lin Chuchu, Tang Tianxiu, and Li Junpan, these first-class actors, and with Wu Yonggang, one of the most promising directors, directing, it is enough to prove how excellent this play is.

What is even more noteworthy is the new child star Ge Zuozhi in this film, because of his excellent achievements in "Black Heart Charm," Lianyi specifically invited him from Hong Kong to contribute to the success of this play.

"Little Angel" is a story of the joys and sorrows of a small world, with extremely strong emotions, even the most subtle accidents, but occurring in this small world, will have extremely great moving power.

Indeed, in this play, Wang Renmei's loving affection between siblings will move people to tears.

You will immediately feel that this is the noblest and most authentic emotion of mankind.

"Little Angel" is a play with the most authentic emotions and noble sentiments.
