SHEN BAO LOCAL SUPPLEMENT AUTOMOBILE WEEKLY

DEATH OF FRENCH AUTOMOBILE KING CITROËN

— (Shadow Idiot)

French automobile king M. Andre Citroën passed away suddenly in a hospital in Paris on July 3rd of this year. The news was transmitted, and it truly caused people in the automotive industry throughout the world to express their sorrow. Citroën was only 57 years old. Not a very old age. In theory, he could have lived for several more years. He had been suffering from his illness for quite some time. Until recently, it was due to stomach cancer. After the doctor performed surgery, unexpectedly, it resulted in his passing away. Citroën's death not only caused a major blow to the French business world, but even had a considerable impact on the whole of Europe. Because after the European War, Citroën himself truly made great contributions to the business world. When we think back, at the end of last December, the Citroën factory he founded was, for a time, ineffective due to the impact of the economic downturn. There was news of an impending liquidation. Later, the government provided assistance, so it was able to overcome the difficulties and avoid bankruptcy. Who knew that not long after, although the Citroën factory is now operating reluctantly, the owner, Citroën, passed away. His death is undoubtedly a major loss for the French automotive industry.

Citroën was born on February 5, 1878. In his early years, he received military training in the heavy artillery and engineering corps. At that time, he was indeed a student to be noted. His success in military school enabled him to serve in the army after graduation. But although he was a promising military man, in his heart, he very much wanted to take a chance in the business world and independently establish a factory.

After completing his term of service in the heavy artillery corps, he began to establish a small factory in 1901, manufacturing the "Citroën Conveyor." This machine was invented by him himself. Initially, his small factory only employed ten workers and one pattern maker. He himself held several positions as designer, technician, business operator, and director. He was extremely busy, but his enterprise had already achieved considerable success from the beginning. In 1908, he joined the Mors factory's board of directors, reorganized the Mors factory, and affiliated it with the Citroën company. Even the production methods and market promotion were completely changed. As a result, his products soon increased tenfold in sales, and he himself gained many important experiences at that time.

Later, the European War broke out. He served in the 82nd Heavy Artillery Corps of the Army and had already obtained the rank of lieutenant. In 1915, he announced a plan for mass-producing munitions. Two months later, he founded a gunpowder factory in the Joefre area. That factory was affiliated with the Citroën Corporation, a very large factory. It could manufacture 50,000 shells every day. Soon, it increased to 55,000 shells. At the same time, he also contributed two new systems: the distribution of coal and the control of bread.

After the European War ended and the Treaty of Versailles was signed, he began to manufacture 10-horsepower Citroën cars. At first, in order to make it popular, the manufacturing method was very simple. By 1919, his car factory could already manufacture 30 cars a day. In 1924, it was 400 cars a day. In 1930, it was 600 cars. In 1933, it was 1,000 cars. At that time, he adopted a promotional method that was entirely sold by independent distributors. Their vehicles had showrooms everywhere. In addition, he worked hard on advertising. Whether it was on walls or on walkways, there were advertisements for the Citroën factory everywhere. In his lifelong career, the most worthy of our praise was that he had funded three expeditions, allowing them to complete their work in the study of natural science.

In 1933, the Citroën factory introduced a completely new type of car chassis, but from March 1934, the factory's economic situation was very difficult, almost to the point of bankruptcy. In December of the same year, there was even talk of liquidation. Fortunately, government assistance was obtained, so they were able to overcome the difficulties. Since then, the Citroën factory has been reorganized again, reducing its scope, saving expenses, and operating reluctantly. But recently, his death has made the future of the Citroën factory even gloomier. Of course, it is a major loss for the French automotive industry.

OVERSEAS AUTOMOBILE NEWS SUMMARY

— Yu

Gutelich Creates Bulletproof Tires - The police departments and law enforcement agencies of various countries, as well as various automobiles used in military affairs, in addition to having the general special qualities and advantages, also need the function of being bulletproof. Automobiles used in this way travel at very high speeds. Therefore, solid tires are often unsuitable. The tires needed for these vehicles, in addition to having the resilience of pneumatic tires, must also have materials that can resist punctures. The Gutelich Company is a master in manufacturing tires. They have now created a new type of sponge rubber filling. All the points required in these situations can be satisfactorily addressed. After unexpectedly being hit by gunfire, these tires using rubber filling cannot be completely useless. Because there are only a few small air pockets in the punctured area, the remaining sponge can still generate elastic force towards the wheel rim to support the entire vehicle. Therefore, unless the entire tire is completely ruptured and damaged and this sponge rubber filling no longer exists, the operation of the tire will not be affected.

More Tourists Visiting Quebec - According to statistics from the Quebec Provincial Tourism Bureau in Canada, the number of tourists traveling to Quebec has increased. This is enough to show that the reason why Americans tend to go to Canada is not because of the issue of unrestricted alcohol, which is just a coincidence. In the summer of 1934, when the United States first opened its alcohol ban, there were 370,000 cars traveling from the United States to Quebec Province. Other transportation methods such as trains, ships, and buses were also more successful than in 1933. Currently, the highways in Quebec Province are said to have reached 16,000 kilometers. This is also a reason for the increase in tourists.

Production Volume of Williams Wowland Cars - The Williams Wowland factory in Toledo, USA, has recently greatly increased the number of cars it manufactures. According to Mr. Achu, the sales manager of the factory, the factory produced 7,500 cars in 1934. But in the first seven months of 1935, its production volume could reach 18,000 cars. This number will double compared to 1934. It is also reported that the factory will produce another 10,000 cars in the coming months.

General Motors Earns Profit - In the second quarter of this year, the net profit adjusted by General Motors was US$49,925,000, totaling US$1.17 per common share. At the same time last year, it was US$37,973,000, or $0.88 per share. The net profit earned by General Motors in the first six months of this year totaled US$79,141,000, with earnings per share of US$1.85. At the same time in 1934, it was US$64,998,000, with earnings of US$1.51 per share. The value of General Motors cars sold in the second quarter of 1935 was US$343,209,000, while it was US$309,706,000 at the same time in 1934. The value of vehicles sold in the first half of this year was US$594,884,000. At the same time last year, it was US$519,678,000. On June 30, 1935, General Motors' liquid assets were US$340,667,000. On June 30 of last year, it was US$299,838,000.

Serving Packard for Twenty-Five Years - The Packard Motor Company in the United States gives a gold pin as a souvenir to those who have continuously served at the factory for twenty-five years. Recently, another twenty-nine people at the company were qualified to wear the golden pin on their lapels because of their long years of service. These twenty-nine people included President Alvin Macauley. They all completed this long period of service on January 1 of last year. On the day of his 25th anniversary of service to the company, Macauley congratulated the others who had also completed 25 years of service and personally awarded each of them a long-awaited 25-year service commemorative pin. In addition to everyone congratulating each other, other automobile company officials and industry leaders celebrated Macauley's achievement. According to Packard Company's historical records, there are a total of 236 employees who have worked continuously for 25 years. There are 528 people who have worked continuously for 20 years. Employees who have served at the factory for more than five years account for approximately 44% of the total number of employees.

Como Truck Experienced Vicissitudes - In order to achieve excellence in manufacturing and to adapt to the special needs of various regions, the Como factory often sends specialists to investigate and study in various regions. Then, the results of the investigation are used to manufacture suitable automobiles. Therefore, the cargo trucks they sell in Patagonia, New Zealand, and Siberia are slightly different in manufacturing. During the Great War, the British military requisitioned various cargo trucks in the country for military use, stopping transportation outside. Later, the British army obtained a German cargo truck on the Western Front. They discovered that it was a Como brand and immediately investigated it. It turned out that the truck was sold by the Rodong factory to the Russian military in 1912. It was seized by the Germans in East Prussia and used within France. After a certain period of time, it returned to the hands of the British and was used to attack their enemies. This Como truck can be said to have experienced vicissitudes. And its durability cannot be ignored.

DRIVING NOTES ON THE SHANGHAI-GUANGDONG HIGHWAY

There is a gentleman from Fujian, Ni Tuosheng, who recently accompanied two friends on a long-distance trip in his own Y-type small Ford car to investigate the actual development of the highway along the way. First, they departed from Shanghai and reached Hangzhou via the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway. Then, from Hangzhou, they went via Yushan, Nanchang, Changsha, Hengshan, Ganzhou, Dayu, Nanxiong to Shaoguan, then turned to Shantou and arrived in Guangzhou. The journey from Shanghai to Shaoguan was 1,023 miles. From Shaoguan via Shantou to Guangzhou, it was 756 miles. The two totaled 1,779 miles. The travel time was 57 hours for the Shanghai to Shaoguan section. The Shaoguan via Shantou to Guangzhou section was 65 hours. A total of 122 hours. The latter section was shorter, but it took longer than the previous section. This is because it is rugged and difficult to travel between Shantou and Guangzhou, and it is necessary to detour. A total of 106 gallons of gasoline were used on this trip. Except for the round trip between Nanchang and Changsha, and the extra consumption due to many stops along the way, the average was about 24 miles per gallon. According to Mr. Ni, the roads traveled on this trip were all recently built. The highways in Hunan are scientifically based everywhere, neat, solid, and the best in all provinces. Even compared to Europe and the United States, there is not much difference. It is heard that Mr. Ni plans to travel to Guizhou after the autumn cools down. Although our country has been working hard to build highways recently, there are still not many people who drive long distances. Mr. Ni's perseverance is admirable. Another noteworthy thing is that before departure, Mr. Ni had the small Ford car, which was to be used for this long-distance trip, inspected and repaired by the repairman. He did not initially tell them the purpose of the trip. The repairmen only followed the procedures and repaired it once. When they arrived in Guangzhou safely, there were no mechanical problems. Those who heard this were surprised. Therefore, Mr. Ni is very satisfied with the durability and stability of Ford cars. The thoughtful and tireless service of Ford dealerships everywhere is also noteworthy.
